"int" })); }; // typeTouched wird nicht gespeichert; nach Add erneut aus Plan vorbelegen
  const { undo, trigger: triggerUndo, doUndo } = useUndoDelete(setData);
  const remove = (id) => {
    const item = data.runLog.find((r) => r.id === id);
    setData((d) => ({ ...d, runLog: d.runLog.filter((r) => r.id !== id) }));
    if (item) triggerUndo("Lauf", "runLog", item);
  };
  // V3: 5K-Prognose nur aus Qualitäts-Efforts — Easy/Lange bewusst ausgeschlossen,
  // bei Intervallen/Tempo zählen nur die Arbeitsrunden aus den CSV-Splits (Pausen rausgerechnet)
  const predData = useMemo(() => {
    const preds = data.runLog
      .map((r) => { const q = qualityEffort(r); const pred = q ? riegel5k(q.dist, q.sec) : null; return pred ? { iso: r.date, date: fmtISOshort(r.date), pred, basis: q.basis, dist: q.dist, pace: q.sec / q.dist } : null; })
      .filter(Boolean).sort((a, b) => a.iso.localeCompare(b.iso));
    let best = Infinity, bestInfo = null; const trend = [];
    // v6.2: die Bestwert-Linie wird über die VOLLSTÄNDIGE Historie berechnet — der Zeitraum-Filter
    // schneidet erst danach zu, sonst würde ein außerhalb des Fensters liegender Rekord verloren gehen
    // und die Linie fälschlich neu bei 0 anfangen. iso bleibt deshalb an trend/raw erhalten.
    preds.forEach((p) => { const isRecord = p.pred < best; if (isRecord) { best = p.pred; bestInfo = p; } trend.push({ iso: p.iso, date: p.date, pred: best, isRecord }); });
    const raw = preds.map((p) => ({ iso: p.iso, date: p.date, pred: p.pred }));
    return { trend, raw, bestInfo };
  }, [data.runLog]);
  const [predRange, setPredRange] = useState("all");
  const predTrend = useMemo(() => applyTimeRange(predData.trend, predRange), [predData.trend, predRange]);
  const predRaw = useMemo(() => applyTimeRange(predData.raw, predRange), [predData.raw, predRange]);
  const bestInfo = predData.bestInfo;
  const [predView, setPredView] = useState("best"); // "best" = Bestwert-Verlauf, "raw" = Prognose pro Lauf
  const bestPred = bestInfo ? bestInfo.pred : null;
  // Bestzeiten: schnellste effektive Pace je Lauftyp (Intervalle/Tempo = Arbeitsrunden-Pace)
  const pbs = useMemo(() => { const m = {}; data.runLog.forEach((r) => { const p = effectivePace(r); if (!m[r.type] || p < m[r.type].p) m[r.type] = { p, r }; }); return m; }, [data.runLog]);
  const pbIds = useMemo(() => new Set(Object.values(pbs).filter((e) => data.runLog.filter((x) => x.type === e.r.type).length >= 2).map((e) => e.r.id)), [pbs, data.runLog]);
  const confirmPending = () => {
    if (!pending) return;
    const key = `${pending.date}|${pending.dist.toFixed(1)}`;
    const exists = data.runLog.some((r) => `${r.date}|${r.dist.toFixed(1)}` === key);
    if (exists) { setImportMsg({ ok: false, text: "Für dieses Datum und diese Distanz existiert bereits ein Eintrag." }); return; }
    const { laps, typeTouched, ...rest } = pending; // typeTouched ist nur UI-Zustand, wird nicht gespeichert
    const entry = { id: uid(), imported: true, ...rest, ...(laps && laps.length > 1 ? { laps } : {}) };
    setData((d) => ({ ...d, runLog: [...d.runLog, entry] }));
    setImportMsg({ ok: true, text: `Lauf vom ${fmtISOshort(pending.date)} übernommen${laps?.length > 1 ? ` (inkl. ${laps.length} Runden-Splits)` : ""}.` });
    setPending(null);
  };
  const discardPending = () => { setPending(null); setImportMsg(null); };
  // v3.3: Herkunft des Typ-Vorschlags für die Vorschau-Karte (Plan-Treffer vs. Pace-Schätzung)
  const pendingAssign = pending ? assignRunType(pending.date, pending.pace, pending.dist, pending.sec, data.illnessLog, data.planEndMode) : null;

  const handleCsv = (file) => {
    if (!file) return;
    Papa.parse(file, {
      header: true, skipEmptyLines: true,
      complete: (res) => {
        try {
          const rows = res.data || [];
          if (!rows.length) { setImportMsg({ ok: false, text: "Die Datei enthält keine Daten." }); return; }
          const fields = (res.meta && res.meta.fields) || Object.keys(rows[0]);
          const hasDateCol = fields.some((f) => /datum|date/i.test(f));

          // ---- Fall A: Aktivitäten-Liste (mehrere Läufe, mit Datumsspalte) ----
          if (hasDateCol) {
            const parsed = [];
            rows.forEach((row) => {
              const actType = pickCol(row, ["aktivitätstyp", "activity type", "typ", "sport"]);
              if (actType && !/lauf|run|jog/i.test(String(actType))) return; // nur Läufe übernehmen
              const date = parseGarminDate(pickCol(row, ["datum", "date"]));
              const distRaw = pickCol(row, ["distanz", "distance", "strecke"]);
              const timeRaw = pickCol(row, ["zeit", "time", "dauer", "duration"]);
              if (!date || !distRaw) return;
              const dist = parseNumberLoose(distRaw);
              const sec = parseTimeToSec(timeRaw);
              if (!dist || isNaN(dist) || !sec) return;
              const pace = sec / dist;
              const a = assignRunType(date, pace, dist, sec, data.illnessLog, data.planEndMode); // v3.3: Plan gewinnt, Pace nur Fallback
              parsed.push({ date, dist: Math.round(dist * 100) / 100, sec, pace, type: a.type, _assign: a, ...extractExtras(row) });
            });
            if (parsed.length) {
              setData((d) => {
                const exists = new Set(d.runLog.map((r) => `${r.date}|${r.dist.toFixed(1)}`));
                const freshRaw = parsed.filter((p) => !exists.has(`${p.date}|${p.dist.toFixed(1)}`));
                // Statistik bewusst nur über tatsächlich importierte Läufe (Duplikate zählen nicht mit)
                const withExtras = freshRaw.filter((p) => p.hrAvg).length;
                const fromPlan = freshRaw.filter((p) => p._assign.source === "plan").length;
                const byPace = freshRaw.length - fromPlan;
                const mismatchDates = freshRaw.filter((p) => p._assign.mismatch).map((p) => fmtISOshort(p.date));
                const fresh = freshRaw.map(({ _assign, ...p }) => ({ id: uid(), imported: true, ...p }));
                const typeBits = !fresh.length ? ""
                  : fromPlan
                    ? ` Lauftyp bei ${fromPlan === fresh.length ? "allen" : fromPlan} aus dem Trainingsplan übernommen${byPace ? `, bei ${byPace} per Pace geschätzt (kein Plan-Lauf an dem Tag)` : ""}.`
                    : ` Lauftyp per Pace geschätzt — an diesen Tagen steht kein Lauf im Plan.`;
                setImportMsg({ ok: true, text: `${fresh.length} Läufe importiert (${parsed.length - fresh.length} Duplikate übersprungen).${typeBits}${withExtras ? ` Bei ${withExtras} wurden zusätzlich Herzfrequenz-/Höhendaten übernommen.` : ""}${mismatchDates.length ? ` ⚠️ Bitte prüfen (${mismatchDates.join(", ")}): Das gelaufene Tempo passt nicht recht zum geplanten Lauftyp — Typ ggf. im Eintrag anpassen.` : ""}` });
                return { ...d, runLog: [...d.runLog, ...fresh] };
              });
              return;
            }
            // Datumsspalte vorhanden, aber nichts brauchbares gefunden -> unten mit Fall B weiterprobieren
          }

          // ---- Fall B: Garmin-Einzelaktivitäts-/Rundenexport (Warm-up/Laufabschnitte/Cool-Down, ohne Datum) ----
          const summaryRow = findSummaryRow(rows) || rows[rows.length - 1];
          const distRaw = pickCol(summaryRow, ["distanz", "distance"]);
          const timeRaw = pickCol(summaryRow, ["gesamtzeit", "zeit", "time", "duration"]);
          const dist = parseNumberLoose(distRaw);
          const sec = parseTimeToSec(timeRaw);
          if (dist && sec && !isNaN(dist)) {
            const pace = sec / dist;
            const assigned = assignRunType(todayISO(), pace, dist, sec, data.illnessLog, data.planEndMode); // v3.3: Plan gewinnt, Pace nur Fallback
            const distR = Math.round(dist * 100) / 100;
            const extras = extractExtras(summaryRow);
            const laps = extractLaps(rows);
            setPending({ date: todayISO(), type: assigned.type, typeTouched: false, dist: distR, sec, pace, laps, ...extras });
            const bits = [];
            if (extras.hrAvg) bits.push(`Ø ${extras.hrAvg} bpm`);
            if (laps.length > 1) bits.push(`${laps.length} Runden-Splits`);
            setImportMsg({ ok: true, text: `Einzelaktivität erkannt (Rundenexport ohne Datum): ${distR} km in ${secToMMSS(sec)}${bits.length ? " · " + bits.join(" · ") : ""}. Vorschau unten prüfen — Datum setzen und übernehmen.` });
            return;
          }
          setImportMsg({ ok: false, text: "Keine Lauf-Daten gefunden. Unterstützt werden Garmin-Aktivitätenlisten (mit Datumsspalte) und Garmin-Einzelaktivitäts-/Rundenexporte (mit \u201eÜbersicht\u201c-Zeile)." });
        } catch (_) { setImportMsg({ ok: false, text: "Datei konnte nicht gelesen werden." }); }
      },
      error: () => setImportMsg({ ok: false, text: "Datei konnte nicht gelesen werden." }),
    });
  };

  // v6.0: je Lauf der auswertungs-relevante Abschnitt (runEffort) — Pace UND Puls, für die Typ-Charts
  const fullSeries = useMemo(() => data.runLog.filter((r) => r.type === type).sort((a, b) => a.date.localeCompare(b.date)).map((r) => {
    const e = runEffort(r);
    const fastest = r.type === "int" && r.laps ? (classifyLaps(r.laps) || {}).fastest : null;
    return { iso: r.date, date: fmtISOshort(r.date), pace: Math.round(e ? e.pace : r.pace), hr: e && e.hr ? Math.round(e.hr) : (r.hrAvg || null), basis: e ? e.basis : null, fastest: fastest || null };
  }), [data.runLog, type]);
  const [typeRange, setTypeRange] = useState("all");
  const series = useMemo(() => applyTimeRange(fullSeries, typeRange), [fullSeries, typeRange]);
  const effWNow = effectiveWeek(currentWeek, data.illnessLog);
  const target = targetPaceSec(type, effWNow);
  const hrTarget = hrTargetForType(type, effWNow);
  const list = [...data.runLog].sort((a, b) => b.date.localeCompare(a.date)).slice(0, 8);
  // v7.2: Kadenz/Schrittlänge auf Arbeitsabschnitt umgestellt (wie Pace-HF/VO2max weiter unten) — ohne
  // Runden-Import (manueller Eintrag, Aktivitätenliste) fällt runEffort() auf die Gesamtwerte zurück.
  const economySeries = useMemo(() => data.runLog
    .map((r) => { const e = runEffort(r); const cadence = e && e.cadence != null ? e.cadence : r.cadence; const stride = e && e.strideLen != null ? e.strideLen : (r.strideLen ?? null); return cadence ? { iso: r.date, date: fmtISOshort(r.date), type: r.type, cadence, stride } : null; })
    .filter(Boolean)
    .sort((a, b) => a.iso.localeCompare(b.iso)), [data.runLog]);
  // V3: Pace-HF-Verhältnis & VO2max-Schätzung — nur ruhige Läufe (Easy/Lang/Tempo-Block); Intervalle verzerren (HF-Trägheit)
  const hrMax = hrMaxTanaka(Number(data.nutrition?.profile?.age) || 18);
  // v7.0: Arbeitsabschnitt für ALLE Steady-Typen (nicht nur Tempo) — Gesamt-Pace/-HF inkl. Warm-up/
  // Cool-down verfälschte Pace-HF-Verhältnis und VO₂max bei Easy/Langen Läufen (Nutzer-Befund).
  const steadyPoints = useMemo(() => data.runLog
    .filter((r) => r.hrAvg && STEADY_RUN(r) && r.dist >= 1.5)
    .sort((a, b) => a.date.localeCompare(b.date))
    .map((r) => { const e = runEffort(r); return { iso: r.date, date: fmtISOshort(r.date), type: r.type, pace: e ? e.pace : r.pace, hr: e && e.hr ? e.hr : r.hrAvg }; }), [data.runLog]);
  const efSeries = useMemo(() => steadyPoints.map((p) => ({ iso: p.iso, date: p.date, type: p.type, ef: efMetersPerBeat(p.pace, p.hr) })).filter((p) => p.ef), [steadyPoints]);
  const vo2Series = useMemo(() => {
    const pts = steadyPoints.map((p) => { const est = estimateVo2max(p.pace, p.hr, hrMax); return est ? { iso: p.iso, date: p.date, est } : null; }).filter(Boolean);
    return pts.map((p, i, a) => ({ ...p, trend: Math.round(median(a.slice(Math.max(0, i - 4), i + 1).map((x) => x.est)) * 10) / 10 }));
  }, [steadyPoints, hrMax]);
  const vo2Now = vo2Series.length ? vo2Series[vo2Series.length - 1].trend : null;
  const vo2Arrow = useMemo(() => {
    if (vo2Series.length < 2) return "";
    const last = vo2Series[vo2Series.length - 1];
    const old = [...vo2Series].reverse().find((p) => p.iso <= isoAddDays(last.iso, -21));
    if (!old) return "";
    return last.trend - old.trend >= 1 ? "↑" : old.trend - last.trend >= 1 ? "↓" : "→";
  }, [vo2Series]);
  return (
    <div className="space-y-4">
      {/* V3: 5K-Prognose — nur Qualitäts-Efforts */}
      <Card className="p-4" style={{ background: "linear-gradient(135deg,#312e81 0%,#4f46e5 100%)", borderColor: "transparent" }}>
        <Eyebrow color="#c7d2fe">5K-Prognose · Riegel-Formel</Eyebrow>
        {bestPred ? (
          <>
            <div className="mt-1 flex items-baseline gap-2.5">
              <span className="font-num text-3xl font-bold text-white leading-none">{secToMMSS(bestPred)}</span>
              <span className="text-indigo-200 text-xs font-num">≈ {secToMMSS(Math.round(bestPred / 5))}/km</span>
            </div>
            <div className="text-[11px] text-indigo-200 mt-1.5 font-num">Basis: {bestInfo.basis} · {bestInfo.dist} km @ {secToMMSS(Math.round(bestInfo.pace))}/km ({bestInfo.date})</div>
            {vo2Now && <div className="text-[11px] text-indigo-200 mt-0.5">Fitness-Trend: VO₂max ≈ {vo2Now} {vo2Arrow}</div>}
            {predData.trend.length >= 2 && (
              <>
                <div className="flex items-center gap-1 mt-2 mb-1">
                  <button onClick={() => setPredView("best")} className={`text-[10px] px-2 py-0.5 rounded-full font-medium transition ${predView === "best" ? "bg-white text-indigo-700" : "bg-white/15 text-indigo-100"}`}>Bestwert</button>
                  <button onClick={() => setPredView("raw")} className={`text-[10px] px-2 py-0.5 rounded-full font-medium transition ${predView === "raw" ? "bg-white text-indigo-700" : "bg-white/15 text-indigo-100"}`}>Pro Lauf</button>
                  <span className="ml-auto"><TimeRangeSelect value={predRange} onChange={setPredRange} light /></span>
                </div>
                {(predView === "best" ? predTrend : predRaw).length >= 2 ? (
                  <div style={{ width: "100%", height: 100 }}><ResponsiveContainer>
                    <LineChart data={predView === "best" ? predTrend : predRaw} margin={{ top: 4, right: 6, left: -4, bottom: 0 }}>
                      <XAxis dataKey="date" tick={{ fontSize: 9, fill: "#a5b4fc" }} axisLine={false} tickLine={false} interval="preserveStartEnd" />
                      <YAxis reversed domain={["dataMin - 20", "dataMax + 20"]} tickFormatter={secToMMSS} tick={{ fontSize: 9, fill: "#a5b4fc" }} width={46} axisLine={false} tickLine={false} />
                      <Tooltip formatter={(v) => [secToMMSS(v), predView === "best" ? "Bestwert" : "Prognose"]} {...tipTop(true)} />
                      <Line type={predView === "best" ? "stepAfter" : "linear"} dataKey="pred" stroke="#fff" strokeWidth={2.5} dot={predView === "best" ? (p) => (p.payload.isRecord ? <circle key={p.payload.date} cx={p.cx} cy={p.cy} r={2.5} fill="#fff" /> : null) : { r: 2.5, fill: "#fff" }} />
                    </LineChart>
                  </ResponsiveContainer></div>
                ) : <div className="py-4 text-center text-[11px] text-indigo-200/70">Zu wenig Läufe in diesem Zeitraum.</div>}
                <div className="text-[10px] text-indigo-200/70 mt-1">{predView === "best" ? "Zeigt deinen bisher schnellsten Prognosewert — bleibt flach, solange kein neuer Rekord dazukommt." : "Zeigt die Prognose jedes einzelnen Qualitäts-Laufs, auch wenn sie schlechter als dein Bestwert war."}</div>
              </>
            )}
            <div className="text-[10px] text-indigo-200/80 mt-1.5 leading-relaxed">Zählt nur echte Qualitäts-Efforts: 5K-Test, Tempo-Block, Intervall-Arbeitsrunden (Pausen rausgerechnet). Easy/Lange fließen bewusst nicht ein.</div>
          </>
        ) : (
          <div className="text-xs text-indigo-200 mt-1.5 leading-relaxed">Noch keine Qualitätseinheit erfasst. Die Prognose nutzt bewusst nur Intervalle/Tempo (Arbeitsrunden aus dem Garmin-Import) oder den 5K-Test — Easy-Läufe sagen nichts über deine Rennzeit aus und bleiben draußen.</div>
        )}
      </Card>

      {/* Garmin-Import */}
      <Card className="p-4" style={panel(dark, "#6366f1", "#eef2ff", "#c7d2fe")}>
        <div className="flex items-start gap-2">
          <Upload size={15} className="text-indigo-500 mt-0.5 shrink-0" />
          <p className="text-xs text-indigo-900 leading-relaxed"><b>Garmin-Import.</b> Exportiere in Garmin Connect deine Aktivitäten (oder eine Einzelaktivität mit Runden) als CSV und lade sie hier hoch. Neben Datum, Distanz und Zeit werden — sofern vorhanden — auch Herzfrequenz, Schrittfrequenz, Höhenmeter und Runden-Splits übernommen. Der Lauftyp wird automatisch aus deinem Trainingsplan übernommen (Datum → geplante Einheit); nur wenn dort kein Lauf steht, wird er anhand der Pace geschätzt.</p>
        </div>
        <input ref={fileRef} type="file" accept=".csv,text/csv" className="hidden" onChange={(e) => { handleCsv(e.target.files?.[0]); e.target.value = ""; }} />
        <button onClick={() => fileRef.current?.click()} className="mt-2.5 w-full rounded-xl border-2 border-dashed border-indigo-300 bg-white/60 py-2.5 text-sm font-semibold text-indigo-700 flex items-center justify-center gap-1.5"><Upload size={15} /> CSV-Datei auswählen</button>
        {importMsg && <div className={`mt-2 rounded-lg px-2.5 py-1.5 text-[11px] leading-relaxed ${importMsg.ok ? "bg-teal-100 text-teal-800" : "bg-rose-100 text-rose-700"}`}>{importMsg.text}</div>}
      </Card>

      {/* Vorschau eines erkannten Einzellaufs (Rundenexport ohne Datum) */}
      {pending && (
        <Card className="p-4" style={panel(dark, "#f59e0b", "#fffbeb", "#fcd34d")}>
          <Eyebrow color="#b45309">Vorschau · Datum bestätigen</Eyebrow>
          <div className="mt-2 grid grid-cols-2 gap-2.5">
            <input type="date" value={pending.date} onChange={(e) => setPending((p) => { const nd = e.target.value; const a = assignRunType(nd, p.pace, p.dist, p.sec, data.illnessLog, data.planEndMode); return { ...p, date: nd, ...(p.typeTouched ? {} : { type: a.type }) }; })} className="tc-input col-span-2" />
            <select value={pending.type} onChange={(e) => setPending({ ...pending, type: e.target.value, typeTouched: true })} className="tc-input col-span-2">{RUN_OPTS.map(([v, l]) => <option key={v} value={v}>{l}</option>)}</select>
          </div>
          {pendingAssign && !pending.typeTouched && (
            <div className="mt-2 text-[10.5px] leading-relaxed" style={{ color: safeText(dark, "#92400e") }}>
              {pendingAssign.source === "plan"
                ? `Typ aus dem Trainingsplan übernommen (Woche ${pendingAssign.planInfo.week}, ${DAY_FULL[pendingAssign.planInfo.day]}: ${RUN_TYPE[pendingAssign.planInfo.type].label}).`
                : "An diesem Tag steht kein Lauf im Plan — Typ per Pace geschätzt."}
              {pendingAssign.mismatch && ` ⚠️ Das gelaufene Tempo wirkt eher nach „${RUN_TYPE[pendingAssign.paceGuess].label}“ — bitte kurz prüfen.`}
            </div>
          )}
          <div className="mt-2.5 font-num text-sm text-slate-800">{pending.dist} km · {secToMMSS(pending.sec)} · {secToMMSS(pending.pace)}/km</div>
          <div className="mt-2 flex flex-wrap gap-1.5">
            {pending.hrAvg && <MiniBadge icon={<HeartPulse size={11} />} text={`Ø ${pending.hrAvg} bpm`} color="#e11d48" />}
            {pending.hrMax && <MiniBadge text={`Max ${pending.hrMax} bpm`} color="#e11d48" />}
            {pending.cadence && <MiniBadge text={`${pending.cadence} spm`} color="#0d9488" />}
            {pending.strideLen && <MiniBadge text={`${pending.strideLen} m Schritt`} color="#0d9488" />}
            {pending.elevGain != null && pending.elevGain > 0 && <MiniBadge icon={<Mountain size={11} />} text={`+${pending.elevGain} m`} color="#78350f" />}
            {pending.calories && <MiniBadge text={`${pending.calories} kcal`} color="#7c3aed" />}
            {pending.laps?.length > 1 && <MiniBadge text={`${pending.laps.length} Runden`} color="#4338ca" />}
          </div>
          <div className="mt-3 flex gap-2">
            <button onClick={discardPending} className="flex-1 rounded-xl bg-white border border-amber-300 text-amber-800 py-2 text-xs font-semibold">Verwerfen</button>
            <button onClick={confirmPending} className="flex-1 rounded-xl bg-amber-500 text-white py-2 text-xs font-semibold flex items-center justify-center gap-1.5"><Check size={14} /> Übernehmen</button>
          </div>
        </Card>
      )}

      <Card className="p-4"><Eyebrow color="#4338ca">Zielpace aktuell (Woche {currentWeek})</Eyebrow>
        <div className="mt-2 grid grid-cols-2 gap-2 text-sm">
          <div className="rounded-xl bg-indigo-50 p-2.5"><div className="text-[11px] text-indigo-500 font-semibold">Intervalle</div><div className="font-num font-bold text-indigo-900">{secToMMSS(targetPaceSec("int", effectiveWeek(currentWeek, data.illnessLog)))}/km</div></div>
          <div className="rounded-xl bg-indigo-50 p-2.5"><div className="text-[11px] text-indigo-500 font-semibold">Tempo</div><div className="font-num font-bold text-indigo-900">{secToMMSS(targetPaceSec("tempo", effectiveWeek(currentWeek, data.illnessLog)))}/km</div></div>
        </div>
      </Card>
      <Card className="p-4"><Eyebrow>Lauf manuell eintragen</Eyebrow>
        <div className="mt-3 grid grid-cols-2 gap-2.5">
          <input type="date" value={form.date} onChange={(e) => setForm((f) => { const nd = e.target.value; return { ...f, date: nd, ...(f.typeTouched ? {} : { type: plannedRunFor(nd, data.illnessLog, data.planEndMode)?.type ?? "int" }) }; })} className="tc-input col-span-2" />
          <select value={form.type} onChange={(e) => setForm({ ...form, type: e.target.value, typeTouched: true })} className="tc-input col-span-2">{RUN_OPTS.map(([v, l]) => <option key={v} value={v}>{l}</option>)}</select>
          {(() => { const fp = plannedRunFor(form.date, data.illnessLog, data.planEndMode); return (
            <div className="col-span-2 -mt-1 text-[10.5px] leading-relaxed" style={{ color: safeText(dark, fp ? "#4338ca" : "#94a3b8") }}>
              {fp && !form.typeTouched
                ? `Aus Plan vorbelegt: Woche ${fp.week}, ${DAY_FULL[fp.day]} — ${RUN_TYPE[fp.type].label}. Bei Bedarf oben anpassen.`
                : fp
                  ? `Plan an dem Tag: ${RUN_TYPE[fp.type].label} (du hast den Typ selbst gewählt).`
                  : "Kein Lauf im Plan an dem Tag — Typ frei wählbar."}
            </div>
          ); })()}
          <input inputMode="decimal" placeholder="Distanz (km)" value={form.dist} onChange={(e) => setForm({ ...form, dist: e.target.value })} className="tc-input" />
          <input inputMode="numeric" placeholder="Zeit (mm:ss)" value={form.time} onChange={(e) => setForm({ ...form, time: e.target.value })} className="tc-input font-num" />
        </div>
        <button onClick={add} className="mt-3 w-full rounded-xl bg-indigo-600 text-white py-2.5 text-sm font-semibold flex items-center justify-center gap-1.5"><Plus size={16} /> Hinzufügen</button>
      </Card>
      <Card className="p-4">
        <div className="flex items-center justify-between mb-1 gap-1.5 flex-wrap">
          <Eyebrow>Fortschritt je Lauftyp</Eyebrow>
          <div className="flex items-center gap-1.5">
            <TimeRangeSelect value={typeRange} onChange={setTypeRange} />
            <select value={type} onChange={(e) => setType(e.target.value)} className="text-xs font-semibold text-slate-600 bg-slate-100 rounded-lg px-2 py-1 border-0">{RUN_OPTS.map(([v, l]) => <option key={v} value={v}>{l}</option>)}</select>
          </div>
        </div>
        <div className="text-[10px] text-slate-400 mb-2">Gleiche Pace bei weniger Puls (oder schneller bei gleichem Puls) = bessere Ausdauer{(target || hrTarget.band) ? ` · Band = Plan-Ziel (Woche ${effWNow})` : ""}</div>
        {series.length >= 2 ? (
          <TypeProgressCharts key={type + typeRange} series={series} target={target} hrTarget={hrTarget} />
        ) : <div className="py-8 text-center text-xs text-slate-400">{fullSeries.length >= 2 ? "Zu wenig Läufe in diesem Zeitraum." : "Mind. 2 Einträge dieser Art für den Verlauf — importiere oben deine Garmin-CSV oder trag Läufe manuell ein."}</div>}
      </Card>

      {/* 2.0: Bestzeiten je Lauftyp */}
      {Object.keys(pbs).length > 0 && (
        <Card className="p-4">
          <Eyebrow>Bestzeiten (Pace)</Eyebrow>
          <div className="mt-2 grid grid-cols-2 gap-2">
            {RUN_OPTS.filter(([v]) => pbs[v]).map(([v, l]) => (
              <div key={v} className="rounded-xl bg-slate-100 p-2.5">
                <div className="text-[11px] font-semibold text-slate-500">{l}</div>
                <div className="font-num font-bold text-slate-800">{secToMMSS(pbs[v].p)}/km</div>
                <div className="text-[10px] text-slate-400 font-num">{fmtISOshort(pbs[v].r.date)} · {pbs[v].r.dist} km</div>
              </div>
            ))}
          </div>
        </Card>
      )}

      {/* v6.2: Laufökonomie/Pace-HF/VO2max konsolidiert (statt drei Cards hintereinander) */}
      <SmartChartsCard economySeries={economySeries} efSeries={efSeries} vo2Series={vo2Series} vo2Now={vo2Now} vo2Arrow={vo2Arrow} hrMax={hrMax} dark={dark} />

      {list.length > 0 && <Card className="divide-y divide-slate-100">{list.map((r) => {
        const hasLaps = r.laps && r.laps.length > 1;
        // v7.2: Pace/Ø HF/Kadenz zeigen jetzt konsequent den Arbeitsabschnitt (wie SplitsChart/Fortschritt
        // je Lauftyp), nicht mehr den Gesamt-Schnitt inkl. Warm-up/Cool-down — bei Läufen ohne Runden
        // (manueller Eintrag, Aktivitätenliste) fällt runEffort() automatisch auf die Gesamtwerte zurück.
        const eff = runEffort(r);
        const dispPace = eff ? eff.pace : r.pace;
        const dispHr = eff && eff.hr != null ? eff.hr : r.hrAvg;
        const dispCadence = eff && eff.cadence != null ? eff.cadence : r.cadence;
        const showTotalPace = Math.round(dispPace) !== Math.round(r.pace);
        const hasBadges = dispHr || dispCadence || (r.elevGain != null && r.elevGain > 0) || r.calories;
        const isOpen = openRun === r.id;
        return (
          <div key={r.id}>
            <div className="flex items-center gap-3 px-4 py-2.5">
              <span className="text-[11px] text-slate-400 font-num w-12 shrink-0">{fmtISOshort(r.date)}</span>
              <span className="text-xs font-semibold text-slate-700 w-20 shrink-0">{RUN_TYPE[r.type].label}{pbIds.has(r.id) && <span className="ml-1 text-[9px] font-bold text-amber-500 align-top">PB</span>}{r.imported && <span className="block text-[9px] font-medium text-indigo-400">Garmin</span>}{showTotalPace && <span className="block text-[9px] font-medium text-slate-400 font-num">Gesamt {secToMMSS(Math.round(r.pace))}/km</span>}</span>
              <span className="font-num text-sm text-slate-800">{r.dist} km · {secToMMSS(r.sec)}</span>
              <span className="font-num text-xs text-indigo-600 ml-auto">{secToMMSS(Math.round(dispPace))}/km</span>
              {hasLaps && <button onClick={() => setOpenRun(isOpen ? null : r.id)} className="text-slate-400 p-1 shrink-0"><ChevronDown size={14} className={`transition-transform ${isOpen ? "rotate-180" : ""}`} /></button>}
              <button onClick={() => remove(r.id)} className="text-slate-300 shrink-0"><Trash2 size={14} /></button>
            </div>
            {/* v6.4: bei aufgeklappter Runde liefert SplitsChart bereits präzisere Kennzahlen zum selben
               Lauf (Arbeits-Pace/Ziel-Chips/Drift) — die generische Übersichts-Zeile hier würde nur
               gestapelte, redundante Kopf-Chips erzeugen (Feedback: "voll/unübersichtlich"). */}
            {hasBadges && !isOpen && (
              <div className="flex flex-wrap gap-1.5 px-4 pb-2 -mt-1">
                {dispHr && <MiniBadge icon={<HeartPulse size={10} />} text={`Ø ${dispHr} bpm`} color="#e11d48" />}
                {dispCadence && <MiniBadge text={`${dispCadence} spm`} color="#0d9488" />}
                {r.elevGain != null && r.elevGain > 0 && <MiniBadge icon={<Mountain size={10} />} text={`+${r.elevGain} m`} color="#78350f" />}
                {r.calories && <MiniBadge text={`${r.calories} kcal`} color="#7c3aed" />}
              </div>
            )}
            {hasLaps && isOpen && <SplitsChart laps={r.laps} run={r} illnessLog={data.illnessLog} planEndMode={data.planEndMode} />}
          </div>
        );
      })}</Card>}
      <UndoToast undo={undo} onUndo={doUndo} />
    </div>
  );
}
function StrengthProgress({ data, setData }) {
  const dark = useDark();
  const names = useMemo(() => [...new Set(data.strengthLog.map((s) => s.exercise))], [data.strengthLog]);
  const [view, setView] = useState("");
  const [form, setForm] = useState({ date: todayISO(), exercise: "", weight: "", reps: "", sets: "" });
  useEffect(() => { if (!view && names.length) setView(names[0]); }, [names, view]);
  const add = () => { if (!form.exercise.trim()) return; setData((d) => ({ ...d, strengthLog: [...d.strengthLog, { id: uid(), date: form.date, exercise: form.exercise.trim(), weight: Number(form.weight) || 0, reps: Number(form.reps) || 0, sets: Number(form.sets) || 0 }] })); setForm({ ...form, weight: "", reps: "" }); };
  const { undo, trigger: triggerUndo, doUndo } = useUndoDelete(setData);
  const remove = (id) => {
    const item = data.strengthLog.find((s) => s.id === id);
    setData((d) => ({ ...d, strengthLog: d.strengthLog.filter((s) => s.id !== id) }));
    if (item) triggerUndo("Eintrag", "strengthLog", item);
  };
  const unitOf = (name) => (/sprung|jump/i.test(name || "") ? "cm" : "kg"); // 2.0: Sprunghöhe in cm statt kg
  // v6.2 Motivations-Audit: Laufen hat Bestzeiten-Tiles, Kraft hatte gar keine Bestwerte — nachgezogen
  const strengthPbs = useMemo(() => {
    const m = {};
    data.strengthLog.forEach((s) => { if (s.weight > 0 && (!m[s.exercise] || s.weight > m[s.exercise].weight)) m[s.exercise] = s; });
    return m;
  }, [data.strengthLog]);
  const fullSeries = useMemo(() => data.strengthLog.filter((s) => s.exercise === view && s.weight > 0).sort((a, b) => a.date.localeCompare(b.date)).map((s) => ({ iso: s.date, date: fmtISOshort(s.date), weight: s.weight })), [data.strengthLog, view]);
  const [strengthRange, setStrengthRange] = useState("all");
  const series = useMemo(() => applyTimeRange(fullSeries, strengthRange), [fullSeries, strengthRange]);
  const list = [...data.strengthLog].sort((a, b) => b.date.localeCompare(a.date)).slice(0, 8);
  return (
    <div className="space-y-4">
      <Card className="p-4" style={panel(dark, "#059669", "#ecfdf5", "#a7f3d0")}>
        <div className="flex items-start gap-2"><Info size={15} className="text-emerald-500 mt-0.5 shrink-0" /><p className="text-xs text-emerald-900 leading-relaxed"><b>Noch keine Maximalwerte?</b> Mach einmalig einen Baseline-Test mit sauberer Technik, dann hast du Startwerte zum Vergleichen. Tippe eine Übung zum Vorausfüllen an:</p></div>
        <div className="mt-2.5 flex flex-wrap gap-1.5">{BASELINE.map((b) => <button key={b} onClick={() => setForm({ ...form, exercise: b.replace(/\s*\(.*\)/, "") })} className="rounded-full bg-white border border-emerald-200 px-2.5 py-1 text-[11px] font-medium text-emerald-700">{b}</button>)}</div>
      </Card>
      <Card className="p-4"><Eyebrow>Satz eintragen</Eyebrow>
        <div className="mt-3 grid grid-cols-2 gap-2.5">
          <input type="date" value={form.date} onChange={(e) => setForm({ ...form, date: e.target.value })} className="tc-input col-span-2" />
          <input list="ex-list" placeholder="Übung" value={form.exercise} onChange={(e) => setForm({ ...form, exercise: e.target.value })} className="tc-input col-span-2" />
          <datalist id="ex-list">{["Kniebeuge", "Kreuzheben", "Bankdrücken", "Klimmzüge", "Schulterdrücken", "Rudern", ...names].map((n) => <option key={n} value={n} />)}</datalist>
          <input inputMode="decimal" placeholder="kg" value={form.weight} onChange={(e) => setForm({ ...form, weight: e.target.value })} className="tc-input font-num" />
          <input inputMode="numeric" placeholder="Wdh." value={form.reps} onChange={(e) => setForm({ ...form, reps: e.target.value })} className="tc-input font-num" />
          <input inputMode="numeric" placeholder="Sätze" value={form.sets} onChange={(e) => setForm({ ...form, sets: e.target.value })} className="tc-input font-num col-span-2" />
        </div>
        <button onClick={add} className="mt-3 w-full rounded-xl bg-emerald-600 text-white py-2.5 text-sm font-semibold flex items-center justify-center gap-1.5"><Plus size={16} /> Hinzufügen</button>
      </Card>
      {Object.keys(strengthPbs).length > 0 && (
        <Card className="p-4">
          <Eyebrow>Bestwerte</Eyebrow>
          <div className="mt-2 grid grid-cols-2 gap-2">
            {Object.entries(strengthPbs).map(([ex, s]) => (
              <div key={ex} className="rounded-xl bg-slate-100 p-2.5">
                <div className="text-[11px] font-semibold text-slate-500 truncate">{ex}</div>
                <div className="font-num font-bold text-slate-800">{s.weight} {unitOf(ex)}</div>
                <div className="text-[10px] text-slate-400 font-num">{fmtISOshort(s.date)}{s.reps ? ` · ${s.reps} Wdh.` : ""}</div>
              </div>
            ))}
          </div>
        </Card>
      )}
      <Card className="p-4">
        <div className="flex items-center justify-between mb-2 gap-1.5 flex-wrap">
          <Eyebrow>Gewichtsverlauf</Eyebrow>
          <div className="flex items-center gap-1.5">
            <TimeRangeSelect value={strengthRange} onChange={setStrengthRange} />
            {names.length > 0 && <select value={view} onChange={(e) => setView(e.target.value)} className="text-xs font-semibold text-slate-600 bg-slate-100 rounded-lg px-2 py-1 border-0" style={{ maxWidth: 130 }}>{names.map((n) => <option key={n} value={n}>{n}</option>)}</select>}
          </div>
        </div>
        {series.length >= 2 ? (
          <div style={{ width: "100%", height: 180 }}><ResponsiveContainer>
            <LineChart data={series} margin={{ top: 5, right: 8, left: -4, bottom: 0 }}>
              <CartesianGrid strokeDasharray="3 3" stroke={gridCol(dark)} />
              <XAxis dataKey="date" tick={{ fontSize: 10, fill: "#94a3b8" }} interval="preserveStartEnd" />
              <YAxis domain={["dataMin-5", "dataMax+5"]} tick={{ fontSize: 10, fill: "#94a3b8" }} width={36} />
              <Tooltip formatter={(v) => [v + " " + unitOf(view), unitOf(view) === "cm" ? "Höhe" : "Gewicht"]} {...tipTop(dark)} />
              <Line type="linear" dataKey="weight" stroke="#059669" strokeWidth={2.5} dot={{ r: 3, fill: "#059669" }} />
            </LineChart>
          </ResponsiveContainer></div>
        ) : <div className="py-8 text-center text-xs text-slate-400">{fullSeries.length >= 2 ? "Zu wenig Einträge in diesem Zeitraum." : "Mind. 2 Einträge dieser Übung für den Verlauf."}</div>}
      </Card>
      {list.length > 0 && <Card className="divide-y divide-slate-100">{list.map((s) => (
        <div key={s.id} className="flex items-center gap-3 px-4 py-2.5">
          <span className="text-[11px] text-slate-400 font-num w-12 shrink-0">{fmtISOshort(s.date)}</span>
          <span className="text-xs font-semibold text-slate-700 truncate flex-1">{s.exercise}</span>
          <span className="font-num text-sm text-slate-800 shrink-0">{s.weight ? `${s.weight} ${unitOf(s.exercise)}` : ""}{(s.sets || s.reps) ? `  ${s.sets || "?"}×${s.reps || "?"}` : ""}</span>
          <button onClick={() => remove(s.id)} className="text-slate-300 shrink-0"><Trash2 size={14} /></button>
        </div>
      ))}</Card>}
      <UndoToast undo={undo} onUndo={doUndo} />
    </div>
  );
}

function SyncCard({ data, setData, savedAt, onRefresh, refreshing }) {
  const [open, setOpen] = useState(false);
  const [text, setText] = useState("");
  const [msg, setMsg] = useState(null);
  const fileRef = useRef(null);

  const doExport = () => {
    const json = buildBackupPayload(data);
    const downloaded = downloadBackup(json);
    setText(json);
    let copied = false;
    try { if (navigator.clipboard?.writeText) { navigator.clipboard.writeText(json); copied = true; } } catch (_) {}
    setMsg({ ok: true, text: (downloaded ? "Datei heruntergeladen" : "Datei-Download nicht möglich") + (copied ? " und in die Zwischenablage kopiert." : ".") + " Auf dem anderen Gerät unten bei „Importieren“ einfügen oder die Datei öffnen." });
    setOpen(true);
  };
  const doImportText = () => {
    try {
      const parsed = JSON.parse(text);
      const incoming = parsed && parsed.data ? parsed.data : parsed;
      if (!incoming || typeof incoming !== "object") throw new Error("ungültig");
      setData({ ...DEFAULT_DATA, ...incoming });
      setMsg({ ok: true, text: "Daten übernommen — dieses Gerät ist jetzt auf dem importierten Stand." });
      setText("");
    } catch (_) { setMsg({ ok: false, text: "Konnte den Text nicht als Sicherung lesen. Bitte den vollständigen Export-Text/-Datei verwenden." }); }
  };
  const handleFile = (file) => {
    if (!file) return;
    const reader = new FileReader();
    reader.onload = () => setText(String(reader.result || ""));
    reader.readAsText(file);
  };

  return (
    <Card className="p-4">
      <div className="flex items-center justify-between gap-2">
        <Eyebrow>Geräteübergreifend nutzen</Eyebrow>
        {savedAt && <span className="text-[10px] text-slate-400 font-num shrink-0">gespeichert {savedAt.toLocaleTimeString("de-DE", { hour: "2-digit", minute: "2-digit" })}</span>}
      </div>
      <p className="text-xs text-slate-500 leading-relaxed mt-1.5">
        Deine Daten werden automatisch mit deinem Claude-Konto gespeichert — auf iPhone und iPad mit demselben Konto (und derselben Unterhaltung) siehst du in der Regel denselben Stand. Falls nicht, überträgst du hier per Sicherungsdatei/-text geräteunabhängig.
      </p>
      <div className="mt-3 flex gap-2">
        <button onClick={onRefresh} disabled={refreshing} className="flex-1 rounded-xl bg-slate-100 text-slate-700 py-2.5 text-xs font-semibold flex items-center justify-center gap-1.5 disabled:opacity-50"><RefreshCw size={13} className={refreshing ? "animate-spin" : ""} /> Aktualisieren</button>
        <button onClick={doExport} className="flex-1 rounded-xl bg-indigo-600 text-white py-2.5 text-xs font-semibold flex items-center justify-center gap-1.5"><Download size={13} /> Exportieren</button>
        <button onClick={() => setOpen((o) => !o)} className="flex-1 rounded-xl bg-slate-100 text-slate-700 py-2.5 text-xs font-semibold flex items-center justify-center gap-1.5"><Upload size={13} /> Importieren</button>
      </div>
      {msg && <div className={`mt-2 rounded-lg px-2.5 py-1.5 text-[11px] leading-relaxed ${msg.ok ? "bg-teal-100 text-teal-800" : "bg-rose-100 text-rose-700"}`}>{msg.text}</div>}
      {open && (
        <div className="mt-3 space-y-2">
          <input ref={fileRef} type="file" accept=".json,application/json" className="hidden" onChange={(e) => { handleFile(e.target.files?.[0]); e.target.value = ""; }} />
          <button onClick={() => fileRef.current?.click()} className="w-full rounded-xl border-2 border-dashed border-slate-300 py-2.5 text-xs font-semibold text-slate-600 flex items-center justify-center gap-1.5"><Upload size={13} /> Sicherungsdatei wählen</button>
          <textarea value={text} onChange={(e) => setText(e.target.value)} rows={4} placeholder="…oder Sicherungstext hier einfügen (vom anderen Gerät kopiert)" className="tc-input font-num" style={{ fontSize: 11 }} />
          <button onClick={doImportText} className="w-full rounded-xl bg-teal-600 text-white py-2.5 text-xs font-semibold flex items-center justify-center gap-1.5"><Copy size={13} /> Text übernehmen</button>
        </div>
      )}
    </Card>
  );
}

/* ===================== RECOVERY ===================== */
function Scale({ value, onChange, color }) {
  const dark = useDark();
  return (
    <div className="flex gap-1.5">{[1, 2, 3, 4, 5].map((n) => (
      <button key={n} onClick={() => onChange(n)} className="flex-1 h-9 rounded-lg text-sm font-semibold font-num border transition" style={value === n ? { background: color, color: "#fff", borderColor: color } : (dark ? { background: "#141d2c", color: "#8ea0b5", borderColor: "#31405c" } : { background: "#fff", color: "#94a3b8", borderColor: "#e2e8f0" })}>{n}</button>
    ))}</div>
  );
}
/* v5.0: Krankheit erfassen — markiert betroffene Einheiten, schützt die Serie, verzögert die Plan-Progression */
function IllnessLogCard({ data, setData, triggerUndo }) {
  const dark = useDark();
  const [form, setForm] = useState({ start: todayISO(), end: "", note: "" });
  const log = data.illnessLog || [];
  const save = () => {
    if (!form.start) return;
    const end = form.end ? (form.end >= form.start ? form.end : form.start) : null;
    setData((d) => ({ ...d, illnessLog: [...(d.illnessLog || []), { id: uid(), start: form.start, end, note: form.note.trim() }] }));
    setForm({ start: todayISO(), end: "", note: "" });
  };
  const endNow = (id) => setData((d) => ({ ...d, illnessLog: (d.illnessLog || []).map((e) => (e.id === id ? { ...e, end: todayISO() } : e)) }));
  const remove = (id) => {
    const item = log.find((e) => e.id === id);
    setData((d) => ({ ...d, illnessLog: (d.illnessLog || []).filter((e) => e.id !== id) }));
    if (item) triggerUndo("Krankheits-Eintrag", "illnessLog", item);
  };
  const sorted = [...log].sort((a, b) => b.start.localeCompare(a.start));
  return (
    <Card className="p-4">
      <div className="flex items-center gap-1.5"><Thermometer size={13} className="text-rose-600" /><Eyebrow color="#e11d48">Krank / Trainingspause</Eyebrow></div>
      <p className="text-[11px] text-slate-400 mt-1 mb-2 leading-relaxed">Einheiten in diesem Zeitraum werden als „Krank“ markiert (entschuldigt statt offen), deine Serie bleibt erhalten und der Laufplan steigert sich erst später weiter. Rückwirkendes Eintragen ist ausdrücklich ok. Ohne End-Datum gilt: noch krank.</p>
      <div className="grid grid-cols-2 gap-2.5">
        <div><div className="text-[11px] font-semibold text-slate-500 mb-1.5">Von</div><input type="date" value={form.start} onChange={(e) => setForm({ ...form, start: e.target.value })} className="tc-input font-num" /></div>
        <div><div className="text-[11px] font-semibold text-slate-500 mb-1.5">Bis (optional)</div><input type="date" value={form.end} onChange={(e) => setForm({ ...form, end: e.target.value })} className="tc-input font-num" /></div>
      </div>
      <input placeholder="Notiz (z. B. Erkältung)" value={form.note} onChange={(e) => setForm({ ...form, note: e.target.value })} className="tc-input mt-2.5" />
      <button onClick={save} className="mt-2.5 w-full rounded-xl bg-rose-600 text-white py-2.5 text-sm font-semibold flex items-center justify-center gap-1.5"><Plus size={16} /> Eintragen</button>
      {sorted.length > 0 && (
        <div className="mt-3 space-y-2">
          {sorted.map((e) => (
            <div key={e.id} className="rounded-xl border p-3 flex items-center gap-3" style={{ borderColor: e.end ? (dark ? "#26334a" : "#e2e8f0") : "#e11d4855", background: e.end ? "transparent" : "#e11d48" + (dark ? "1a" : "10") }}>
              <div className="min-w-0 flex-1">
                <div className="text-sm font-semibold text-slate-800 font-num">{fmtISOshort(e.start)} – {e.end ? fmtISOshort(e.end) : "offen"}</div>
                <div className="text-xs text-slate-500 mt-0.5">{e.note || "Krankheit"}{!e.end && <span className="font-semibold text-rose-600"> · noch krank</span>}</div>
              </div>
              {!e.end && <button onClick={() => endNow(e.id)} className="shrink-0 rounded-lg bg-teal-600 text-white px-2.5 py-1.5 text-[11px] font-semibold">Beenden</button>}
              <button onClick={() => remove(e.id)} className="shrink-0 p-1.5 text-slate-300"><Trash2 size={15} /></button>
            </div>
          ))}
        </div>
      )}
    </Card>
  );
}
/* ==== v6.0: eindeutige Zustands-Kodierung für Plan-vs-Ist-Balken ====
   erledigt = satte Füllung · entschuldigt = Schraffur (45°) · offen = fast leer + gestrichelter Umriss.
   Reine Deckkraft-Stufen waren auf dem Handy nicht unterscheidbar. */
function hatchDefs(prefix, dark) {
  return (
    <defs>
      {["vb", "run", "strength"].map((s) => (
        <pattern key={s} id={`${prefix}-${s}`} width="5" height="5" patternUnits="userSpaceOnUse" patternTransform="rotate(45)">
          <rect width="5" height="5" fill={SPORT[s].color} fillOpacity={dark ? 0.26 : 0.18} />
          <line x1="1" y1="0" x2="1" y2="5" stroke={dark ? SPORT[s].bright : SPORT[s].color} strokeWidth="2" strokeOpacity="0.9" />
        </pattern>
      ))}
    </defs>
  );
}
// Cell-Props je Balkensegment: Umrandung für heute/aktuelle Woche gewinnt; offene Segmente mit Wert
// bekommen den gestrichelten Sportfarben-Umriss; leere Segmente bleiben komplett unsichtbar.
function stateCellProps(highlight, openValue, sport, dark) {
  if (highlight) return { stroke: dark ? "#e2e8f0" : "#0f172a", strokeWidth: 1.5 };
  if (openValue > 0) return { stroke: dark ? SPORT[sport].bright : SPORT[sport].color, strokeWidth: 1, strokeDasharray: "3 2", strokeOpacity: 0.9 };
  return { stroke: "none", strokeWidth: 0 };
}
function StateLegend({ dark, extra, showCancelled }) {
  const c = dark ? "#94a3b8" : "#64748b";
  const sw = { display: "inline-block", width: 10, height: 10, borderRadius: 2, verticalAlign: -1 };
  return (
    <div className="flex flex-wrap items-center gap-x-2.5 gap-y-1 text-[10px] text-slate-400 mt-1 mb-1">
      <span className="inline-flex items-center gap-1"><span style={{ ...sw, background: c }} /> erledigt</span>
      <span className="inline-flex items-center gap-1"><span style={{ ...sw, background: `repeating-linear-gradient(45deg, ${c} 0 2px, transparent 2px 5px)` }} /> entschuldigt (krank)</span>
      <span className="inline-flex items-center gap-1"><span style={{ ...sw, border: `1.5px dashed ${c}`, background: "transparent" }} /> offen</span>
      {/* v7.0: eigener Legenden-Eintrag, damit Ausfall nicht mit "offen" verwechselt wird — im Chart
          selbst zusätzlich an der grauen (statt sportfarbenen) Umrandung erkennbar. */}
      {showCancelled && <span className="inline-flex items-center gap-1"><b style={{ color: c }}>✗</b> ausgefallen</span>}
      {extra && <span>· {extra}</span>}
    </div>
  );
}

function RecoveryTab({ data, setData, currentWeek }) {
  const dark = useDark();
  const [form, setForm] = useState({ date: todayISO(), sleep: "", readiness: 0, soreness: 0, note: "", napMin: "", napTime: "frueh_nachmittag", napFeeling: "neutral" });
  const save = () => {
    if (!form.sleep && !form.readiness && !form.napMin) return;
    const hasNap = Number(form.napMin) > 0;
    const entry = {
      id: uid(), date: form.date,
      sleep: Number(String(form.sleep).replace(",", ".")) || 0,
      readiness: form.readiness || 3,
      soreness: form.soreness || 0,
      note: form.note.trim(),
      ...(hasNap ? { napMin: Number(form.napMin), napTime: form.napTime, napFeeling: form.napFeeling } : {}),
    };
    setData((d) => ({ ...d, recoveryLog: [...d.recoveryLog.filter((r) => r.date !== form.date), entry] }));
    setForm({ date: todayISO(), sleep: "", readiness: 0, soreness: 0, note: "", napMin: "", napTime: "frueh_nachmittag", napFeeling: "neutral" });
  };
  const { undo, trigger: triggerUndo, doUndo } = useUndoDelete(setData);
  const remove = (id) => {
    const item = data.recoveryLog.find((r) => r.id === id);
    setData((d) => ({ ...d, recoveryLog: d.recoveryLog.filter((r) => r.id !== id) }));
    if (item) triggerUndo("Check-in", "recoveryLog", item);
  };
  const sorted = [...data.recoveryLog].sort((a, b) => a.date.localeCompare(b.date));
  const recents = [...sorted].reverse();
  const avgSleep = recents.length ? recents.slice(0, 5).reduce((s, r) => s + (r.sleep || 0), 0) / Math.min(5, recents.length) : null;
  const latest = recents[0];
  const weekLoad = plannedWeekLoad(currentWeek, data.vbSlots, data.illnessLog, data.planEndMode, data.overrides);
  const prios = data.prios?.length === 3 ? data.prios : DEFAULT_DATA.prios;
  const status = readinessStatus(weekLoad, avgSleep, latest?.readiness, SPORT[prios[2]].label, napFromEntry(latest));
  const [sleepRange, setSleepRange] = useState("d14"); // Default entspricht dem bisherigen slice(-14)
  const sleepSeries = applyTimeRange(sorted.map((r) => ({ iso: r.date, date: fmtISOshort(r.date), sleep: r.sleep })), sleepRange);
  const tWeek = planWeekOf(TOURNAMENT);
  const weekDays = useMemo(() => {
    const monday = mondayOfWeek(currentWeek);
    return buildWeekPlan(currentWeek, undefined, data.vbSlots, data.illnessLog, data.planEndMode, data.overrides).map((d, i) => {
      // v7.0: ausgefallene Einheiten (load 0, originalLoad>0) gehören mit in die Liste — sonst sieht ein
      // ausgefallenes Volleyball-Training im Tooltip identisch aus wie ein Tag ohne jede geplante Einheit.
      const row = { day: d.day, isToday: isSameDay(new Date(monday.getTime() + i * DAY_MS), new Date()), list: d.items.filter((it) => it.load > 0 || it.cancelled).map((it) => ({ sport: it.sport, label: it.label, load: it.load || 0, done: !!data.done[it.uid], excused: !data.done[it.uid] && it.illness === "sick", cancelled: !!it.cancelled, originalLoad: it.originalLoad || 0 })) };
      ["vb", "run", "strength"].forEach((s) => { row[s + "Done"] = 0; row[s + "Excused"] = 0; row[s + "Open"] = 0; row[s + "Cancelled"] = 0; });
      row.list.forEach((it) => { row[it.sport + (it.cancelled ? "Cancelled" : it.done ? "Done" : it.excused ? "Excused" : "Open")] += it.cancelled ? it.originalLoad : it.load; });
      return row;
    });
  }, [currentWeek, data.vbSlots, data.done, data.illnessLog, data.planEndMode, data.overrides]);
  const totalW = planTotalWeeks(data.illnessLog, data.planEndMode);
  const meso = Array.from({ length: totalW }, (_, i) => {
    const w = i + 1;
    const bySport = weekLoadBySport(w, data.vbSlots, data.illnessLog, data.planEndMode, data.overrides);
    // Erledigt/Entschuldigt je Sportart — nur für vergangene/aktuelle Wochen; Zukunft = reiner Plan (alles "offen")
    const doneBy = { vb: 0, run: 0, strength: 0 }, excusedBy = { vb: 0, run: 0, strength: 0 };
    if (w <= currentWeek) buildWeekPlan(w, undefined, data.vbSlots, data.illnessLog, data.planEndMode, data.overrides).forEach((d) => d.items.forEach((it) => {
      if (doneBy[it.sport] == null) return;
      if (data.done[it.uid]) doneBy[it.sport] += it.load || 0;
      else if (it.illness === "sick") excusedBy[it.sport] += it.load || 0;
    }));
    const effW = w >= totalW ? TOTAL_WEEKS : effectiveWeek(w, data.illnessLog);
    const row = { w: `${w}`, current: w === currentWeek, future: w > currentWeek, kind: w >= totalW ? "Testwoche" : weekMeta(w).hasT ? "Turnierwoche" : REGEN[effW] ? "Regeneration" : "regulär" };
    ["vb", "run", "strength"].forEach((s) => {
      const doneV = Math.min(doneBy[s], bySport[s]);
      const excusedV = Math.min(excusedBy[s], Math.max(bySport[s] - doneV, 0));
      row[s + "Done"] = doneV; row[s + "Excused"] = excusedV; row[s + "Open"] = Math.max(bySport[s] - doneV - excusedV, 0); row[s + "Plan"] = bySport[s];
    });
    return row;
  });

  return (
    <div className="space-y-4">
      <Card className="p-4" style={{ background: dark ? status.color + "21" : status.tint, borderColor: status.color + "55" }}>
        <Eyebrow color={dark ? status.bright : status.color}>Belastungs-Ampel</Eyebrow>
        <div className="mt-1.5 flex items-center gap-3">
          <div className="h-3 w-3 rounded-full shrink-0" style={{ background: dark ? status.bright : status.color }} />
          <div className="font-display font-bold flex items-center gap-1.5 flex-wrap" style={{ color: dark ? status.bright : status.color }}>{status.label}{status.napBoost && <MiniBadge icon={<Moon size={10} />} text="Nap-Boost" color="#7c3aed" />}</div>
        </div>
        <p className="text-xs mt-1.5 leading-relaxed" style={{ color: dark ? status.bright : status.color }}>{status.hint}</p>
        <div className="mt-2.5 flex gap-2 text-[11px]"><span className="rounded-lg bg-white/70 px-2 py-1 font-num text-slate-700">Geplante Belastung Wo. {currentWeek}: ⚡{weekLoad}</span>{avgSleep && <span className="rounded-lg bg-white/70 px-2 py-1 font-num text-slate-700">Schlaf-Ø {avgSleep.toFixed(1)} h</span>}</div>
        <div className="mt-2"><LoadHelp /></div>
      </Card>

      <Card className="p-4">
        <Eyebrow>Täglicher Check-in</Eyebrow>
        <div className="mt-3 space-y-3">
          <div className="grid grid-cols-2 gap-2.5">
            <input type="date" value={form.date} onChange={(e) => setForm({ ...form, date: e.target.value })} className="tc-input" />
            <input inputMode="decimal" placeholder="Schlaf (h)" value={form.sleep} onChange={(e) => setForm({ ...form, sleep: e.target.value })} className="tc-input font-num" />
          </div>
          <div><div className="text-[11px] font-semibold text-slate-500 mb-1.5">Wie fühlst du dich? (1 müde – 5 top)</div><Scale value={form.readiness} onChange={(v) => setForm({ ...form, readiness: v })} color="#0d9488" /></div>
          <div><div className="text-[11px] font-semibold text-slate-500 mb-1.5">Muskelkater (1 keiner – 5 stark)</div><Scale value={form.soreness} onChange={(v) => setForm({ ...form, soreness: v })} color="#f59e0b" /></div>
          <div>
            <div className="text-[11px] font-semibold text-slate-500 mb-1.5">Nap (optional, Minuten)</div>
            <input inputMode="numeric" placeholder="z. B. 20" value={form.napMin} onChange={(e) => setForm({ ...form, napMin: e.target.value })} className="tc-input font-num" />
          </div>
          {Number(form.napMin) > 0 && (
            <div className="rounded-xl bg-slate-100 p-2.5 space-y-2.5">
              <div>
                <div className="text-[11px] font-semibold text-slate-500 mb-1.5">Wann?</div>
                <div className="flex gap-1.5">{NAP_TIMES.map(([v, l]) => (
                  <button key={v} onClick={() => setForm({ ...form, napTime: v })} className={`flex-1 rounded-lg px-1.5 py-2 text-[10.5px] font-semibold border transition ${form.napTime === v ? "bg-violet-600 text-white border-transparent" : "bg-white text-slate-600 border-slate-200"}`}>{l}</button>
                ))}</div>
              </div>
              <div>
                <div className="text-[11px] font-semibold text-slate-500 mb-1.5">Wie gefühlt?</div>
                <div className="flex gap-1.5">{NAP_FEELINGS.map(([v, l]) => (
                  <button key={v} onClick={() => setForm({ ...form, napFeeling: v })} className={`flex-1 rounded-lg px-1.5 py-2 text-[10.5px] font-semibold border transition ${form.napFeeling === v ? "bg-violet-600 text-white border-transparent" : "bg-white text-slate-600 border-slate-200"}`}>{l}</button>
                ))}</div>
              </div>
              {form.napTime === "spaet_nachmittag" && <div className="text-[10.5px] text-amber-700 leading-relaxed">⚠️ Später Nap kann den Nachtschlaf stören — für heute ok, aber nicht zur Gewohnheit werden lassen.</div>}
              <NapHelp />
            </div>
          )}
          <input placeholder="Notiz (optional)" value={form.note} onChange={(e) => setForm({ ...form, note: e.target.value })} className="tc-input" />
          <button onClick={save} className="w-full rounded-xl bg-teal-600 text-white py-2.5 text-sm font-semibold flex items-center justify-center gap-1.5"><Plus size={16} /> Check-in speichern</button>
        </div>
      </Card>

      <IllnessLogCard data={data} setData={setData} triggerUndo={triggerUndo} />

      <Card className="p-4" style={panel(dark, "#14b8a6", "#f0fdfa", "#99f6e4")}>
        <div className="flex items-start gap-2"><Moon size={16} className="text-teal-600 mt-0.5 shrink-0" />
          <div className="text-xs text-teal-900 leading-relaxed">
            <b>Schlaf-Fokus.</b> Aktuell schläfst du oft unter 6 h — das ist dein größter Bremsklotz bei viel Training. Mit 3 Sportarten braucht dein Körper 8–9 h, sonst leiden Anpassung, Sprungkraft und Verletzungsrisiko. <b>Wenig geschlafen?</b> Streiche zuerst die optionale Krafteinheit und halte die harten Läufe locker — eher als sie hart durchzuziehen.
          </div>
        </div>
      </Card>

      <Card className="p-4">
        <div className="flex items-center justify-between"><Eyebrow>Schlaf-Verlauf</Eyebrow><TimeRangeSelect value={sleepRange} onChange={setSleepRange} /></div>
        {sleepSeries.length >= 2 ? (
          <div className="mt-2" style={{ width: "100%", height: 170 }}><ResponsiveContainer>
            <LineChart data={sleepSeries} margin={{ top: 5, right: 8, left: -4, bottom: 0 }}>
              <CartesianGrid strokeDasharray="3 3" stroke={gridCol(dark)} />
              <XAxis dataKey="date" tick={{ fontSize: 10, fill: "#94a3b8" }} interval="preserveStartEnd" />
              <YAxis domain={[0, 10]} tick={{ fontSize: 10, fill: "#94a3b8" }} width={32} />
              <Tooltip formatter={(v) => [v + " h", "Schlaf"]} {...tipTop(dark)} />
              <ReferenceLine y={8} stroke="#14b8a6" strokeDasharray="4 4" label={chipLabel("Ziel 8 h", "#0d9488", dark, chipSide(sleepSeries.map((p) => p.sleep), 8, 10, "below"))} />
              <Line type="linear" dataKey="sleep" stroke="#14b8a6" strokeWidth={2.5} dot={{ r: 3, fill: "#14b8a6" }} />
            </LineChart>
          </ResponsiveContainer></div>
        ) : <div className="py-8 text-center text-xs text-slate-400">{sorted.length >= 2 ? "Zu wenig Check-ins in diesem Zeitraum." : "Mind. 2 Check-ins für den Verlauf."}</div>}
      </Card>

      {/* Diese Woche im Detail: Tag für Tag, gleiche Bildsprache wie der Mesozyklus */}
      <Card className="p-4">
        <Eyebrow>Diese Woche: Plan vs. Ist (Woche {currentWeek})</Eyebrow>
        <StateLegend dark={dark} extra="Umrandung = heute" showCancelled />
        <div style={{ width: "100%", height: 140 }}><ResponsiveContainer>
          <ComposedChart data={weekDays} margin={{ top: 6, right: 4, left: -4, bottom: 0 }}>
            {hatchDefs("hatchWk", dark)}
            <CartesianGrid strokeDasharray="3 3" stroke={gridCol(dark)} vertical={false} />
            <XAxis dataKey="day" tick={{ fontSize: 10, fill: "#94a3b8" }} axisLine={false} tickLine={false} />
            <YAxis tick={{ fontSize: 10, fill: "#94a3b8" }} width={30} allowDecimals={false} />
            <Tooltip {...tipProps(dark)} position={{ y: 0 }} cursor={{ fill: dark ? "#ffffff08" : "#00000006" }} content={({ active, payload }) => {
              if (!active || !payload || !payload.length) return null;
              const d = payload[0].payload;
              return (
                <div style={{ ...tipStyle(dark, 11), padding: "7px 10px", background: dark ? "#16202f" : "#ffffff", border: `1px solid ${dark ? "#2b3950" : "#e2e8f0"}`, borderRadius: 10 }}>
                  <div style={{ fontWeight: 700, marginBottom: 3, color: dark ? "#f8fafc" : "#0f172a" }}>{DAY_FULL[d.day]}</div>
                  {d.list.length ? d.list.map((it, i) => (
                    <div key={i} style={{ color: dark ? "#e2e8f0" : "#0f172a" }}>
                      <span style={{ color: it.cancelled ? (dark ? "#64748b" : "#94a3b8") : safeText(dark, SPORT[it.sport].color) }}>{it.cancelled ? "✗" : it.done ? "✓" : it.excused ? "◐" : "○"}</span> {it.label}{it.cancelled ? " · ausgefallen, zählt nicht" : ` ⚡${it.load}${it.done ? "" : it.excused ? " · entschuldigt (krank)" : " · offen"}`}
                    </div>
                  )) : <div style={{ color: dark ? "#94a3b8" : "#64748b" }}>Ruhetag</div>}
                </div>
              );
            }} />
            {["vb", "run", "strength"].flatMap((s, si) => [
              <Bar key={s + "d"} dataKey={s + "Done"} stackId="a" fill={SPORT[s].color} maxBarSize={26}>{weekDays.map((d, i) => <Cell key={i} {...stateCellProps(d.isToday, 0, s, dark)} />)}</Bar>,
              <Bar key={s + "e"} dataKey={s + "Excused"} stackId="a" fill={`url(#hatchWk-${s})`} maxBarSize={26}>{weekDays.map((d, i) => <Cell key={i} {...stateCellProps(d.isToday, 0, s, dark)} />)}</Bar>,
              // v7.0: eigenes, sportneutral-graues Segment für Ausfälle — bisher fiel die originalLoad
              // komplett raus und der Tag sah aus wie ein nie geplanter Ruhetag.
              <Bar key={s + "c"} dataKey={s + "Cancelled"} stackId="a" fill="none" maxBarSize={26}>{weekDays.map((d, i) => <Cell key={i} stroke={dark ? "#64748b" : "#94a3b8"} strokeWidth={1.2} strokeDasharray="3 2" />)}</Bar>,
              <Bar key={s + "o"} dataKey={s + "Open"} stackId="a" fill={SPORT[s].color} fillOpacity={dark ? 0.12 : 0.09} maxBarSize={26} radius={si === 2 ? [3, 3, 0, 0] : [0, 0, 0, 0]}>{weekDays.map((d, i) => <Cell key={i} {...stateCellProps(d.isToday, d[s + "Open"], s, dark)} />)}</Bar>,
            ])}
          </ComposedChart>
        </ResponsiveContainer></div>
      </Card>

      {/* Wochenbelastung: je Sportart satt = erledigt, blass = offen/geplant */}
      <Card className="p-4">
        <Eyebrow>Wochenbelastung: Plan vs. Ist (Mesozyklus)</Eyebrow>
        <StateLegend dark={dark} extra="Umrandung = aktuelle Woche" />
        <div style={{ width: "100%", height: 170 }}><ResponsiveContainer>
          <ComposedChart data={meso} margin={{ top: 20, right: 4, left: -4, bottom: 0 }}>
            {hatchDefs("hatchMs", dark)}
            <CartesianGrid strokeDasharray="3 3" stroke={gridCol(dark)} vertical={false} />
            <XAxis dataKey="w" tick={{ fontSize: 9, fill: "#94a3b8" }} interval={0} />
            <YAxis tick={{ fontSize: 10, fill: "#94a3b8" }} width={34} />
            <Tooltip {...tipProps(dark)} position={{ y: 0 }} content={({ active, payload, label }) => {
              if (!active || !payload || !payload.length) return null;
              const m = payload[0].payload;
              return (
                <div style={{ ...tipStyle(dark, 11), padding: "7px 10px", background: dark ? "#16202f" : "#ffffff", border: `1px solid ${dark ? "#2b3950" : "#e2e8f0"}`, borderRadius: 10 }}>
                  <div style={{ fontWeight: 700, marginBottom: 3, color: dark ? "#f8fafc" : "#0f172a" }}>Woche {label} · {m.kind}</div>
                  {["vb", "run", "strength"].map((s) => m[s + "Plan"] > 0 && (
                    <div key={s} style={{ color: dark ? "#e2e8f0" : "#0f172a" }}>
                      <span style={{ color: safeText(dark, SPORT[s].color), fontWeight: 600 }}>{SPORT[s].label}:</span> {m.future ? `⚡${m[s + "Plan"]} geplant` : `${m[s + "Done"]} von ${m[s + "Plan"]} ⚡${m[s + "Excused"] ? ` · ${m[s + "Excused"]} entschuldigt` : ""}`}
                    </div>
                  ))}
                </div>
              );
            }} />
            <ReferenceLine x={`${tWeek}`} stroke="#f59e0b" strokeDasharray="4 4" label={chipLabel("Turnier", "#b45309", dark, "vtop")} />
            {["vb", "run", "strength"].flatMap((s, si) => [
              <Bar key={s + "d"} dataKey={s + "Done"} stackId="a" fill={SPORT[s].color}>{meso.map((m, i) => <Cell key={i} {...stateCellProps(m.current, 0, s, dark)} />)}</Bar>,
              <Bar key={s + "e"} dataKey={s + "Excused"} stackId="a" fill={`url(#hatchMs-${s})`}>{meso.map((m, i) => <Cell key={i} {...stateCellProps(m.current, 0, s, dark)} />)}</Bar>,
              <Bar key={s + "o"} dataKey={s + "Open"} stackId="a" fill={SPORT[s].color} fillOpacity={dark ? 0.12 : 0.09} radius={si === 2 ? [3, 3, 0, 0] : [0, 0, 0, 0]}>{meso.map((m, i) => <Cell key={i} {...stateCellProps(m.current, m[s + "Open"], s, dark)} />)}</Bar>,
            ])}
          </ComposedChart>
        </ResponsiveContainer></div>
        <div className="flex flex-wrap gap-2.5 text-[10px] text-slate-500 mt-1">
          {["vb", "run", "strength"].map((s) => <span key={s} className="inline-flex items-center gap-1"><span className="h-2 w-2 rounded-sm" style={{ background: SPORT[s].color }} /> {SPORT[s].label}</span>)}
        </div>
        <div className="mt-2"><LoadHelp /></div>
      </Card>

      {recents.length > 0 && (
        <div><Eyebrow>Letzte Check-ins</Eyebrow>
          <Card className="mt-2 divide-y divide-slate-100">{recents.slice(0, 8).map((r) => (
            <div key={r.id} className="flex items-center gap-3 px-4 py-2.5">
              <span className="text-[11px] text-slate-400 font-num w-12 shrink-0">{fmtISOshort(r.date)}</span>
              <span className="font-num text-sm text-slate-800 shrink-0">{r.sleep}h</span>
              <span className="text-[11px] text-slate-500 shrink-0">Form {r.readiness}/5</span>
              {r.napMin ? <span className="text-[11px] text-violet-500 shrink-0 font-num">😴{r.napMin}m</span> : null}
              {r.note && <span className="text-[11px] text-slate-400 truncate flex-1">{r.note}</span>}
              <button onClick={() => remove(r.id)} className="text-slate-300 ml-auto shrink-0"><Trash2 size={14} /></button>
            </div>
          ))}</Card>
        </div>
      )}
      <UndoToast undo={undo} onUndo={doUndo} />
    </div>
  );
}

/* ===================== V3: ERNÄHRUNG — UI ===================== */
function NutritionProfileForm({ initial, onSave, submitLabel }) {
  const [f, setF] = useState({ ...NUT_DEFAULT.profile, ...initial });
  const plan = kcalPlan(f);
  const set = (k, v) => setF((x) => ({ ...x, [k]: v }));
  const Btn = ({ active, onClick, children, sub }) => (
    <button onClick={onClick} className={`flex-1 rounded-xl px-2 py-2 text-[11px] font-semibold border transition ${active ? "bg-indigo-600 text-white border-transparent" : "bg-white text-slate-600 border-slate-200"}`}>
      <div>{children}</div>{sub && <div className={`text-[9px] font-medium mt-0.5 ${active ? "text-indigo-200" : "text-slate-400"}`}>{sub}</div>}
    </button>
  );
  return (
    <div className="space-y-3.5">
      <div>
        <div className="text-[11px] font-semibold text-slate-500 mb-1.5">Geschlecht (für die Formel)</div>
        <div className="flex gap-1.5">{[["m", "männlich"], ["w", "weiblich"]].map(([v, l]) => <Btn key={v} active={f.sex === v} onClick={() => set("sex", v)}>{l}</Btn>)}</div>
      </div>
      <div className="grid grid-cols-3 gap-2">
        {[["age", "Alter", "Jahre"], ["height", "Größe", "cm"], ["weight", "Gewicht", "kg"]].map(([k, l, u]) => (
          <div key={k}><div className="text-[11px] font-semibold text-slate-500 mb-1.5">{l} <span className="text-slate-400 font-normal">({u})</span></div><input inputMode="decimal" value={f[k]} onChange={(e) => set(k, e.target.value)} className="tc-input font-num" /></div>
        ))}
      </div>
      <div>
        <div className="text-[11px] font-semibold text-slate-500 mb-1.5">Alltagsaktivität (ohne Training — das wird separat angerechnet)</div>
        <div className="flex gap-1.5">{ACTIVITY_LEVELS.map(([v, l, sub]) => <Btn key={v} active={f.activity === v} onClick={() => set("activity", v)} sub={sub}>{l}</Btn>)}</div>
      </div>
      <div>
        <div className="text-[11px] font-semibold text-slate-500 mb-1.5">Ziel</div>
        <div className="flex gap-1.5">{[["cut", "Abnehmen"], ["maintain", "Halten"], ["gain", "Aufbauen"]].map(([v, l]) => <Btn key={v} active={f.goal === v} onClick={() => set("goal", v)}>{l}</Btn>)}</div>
      </div>
      {f.goal !== "maintain" && (
        <div>
          <div className="text-[11px] font-semibold text-slate-500 mb-1.5">Tempo ({f.goal === "cut" ? "kg weniger" : "kg mehr"} pro Woche)</div>
          <div className="flex gap-1.5">{(f.goal === "cut" ? [0.25, 0.5, 0.75] : [0.25, 0.5]).map((v) => <Btn key={v} active={parseNum(f.rate) === v} onClick={() => set("rate", v)}>{String(v).replace(".", ",")} kg</Btn>)}</div>
          {f.goal === "cut" && parseNum(f.rate) >= 0.75 && <div className="text-[10.5px] text-amber-700 mt-1.5 leading-relaxed">0,75 kg/Woche ist mit 3 Sportarten sehr ambitioniert — 0,5 ist meist der bessere Deal zwischen Fortschritt und Trainingsqualität.</div>}
        </div>
      )}
      <div>
        <div className="text-[11px] font-semibold text-slate-500 mb-1.5">Trainings-kcal anrechnen (Garmin-Läufe & manuelle Aktivität)</div>
        <div className="flex gap-1.5">{[[0, "0 %", "konservativ"], [50, "50 %", "empfohlen"], [100, "100 %", "voll"]].map(([v, l, sub]) => <Btn key={v} active={parseNum(f.addBack) === v} onClick={() => set("addBack", v)} sub={sub}>{l}</Btn>)}</div>
      </div>
      <div>
        <div className="text-[11px] font-semibold text-slate-500 mb-1.5">Zielgewicht <span className="text-slate-400 font-normal">(optional, kg)</span></div>
        <input inputMode="decimal" value={f.goalWeight} onChange={(e) => set("goalWeight", e.target.value)} className="tc-input font-num" placeholder="z. B. 72" />
      </div>
      {plan ? (
        <div className="rounded-xl bg-slate-100 p-3 space-y-1">
          <div className="text-[10px] font-semibold text-slate-500 uppercase tracking-widest">Dein Plan</div>
          <div className="flex items-baseline gap-2"><span className="font-num text-2xl font-bold text-slate-900">{plan.target}</span><span className="text-[11px] text-slate-500">kcal/Tag {plan.delta ? `(${plan.delta > 0 ? "+" : ""}${plan.delta})` : "(Erhalt)"}</span></div>
          <div className="text-[10.5px] text-slate-500 font-num">Grundumsatz {plan.bmr} · Alltagsverbrauch {plan.tdee}{plan.calibrated ? " (kalibriert)" : ""} · an Trainingstagen automatisch mehr</div>
          {plan.belowFloor && <div className="text-[10.5px] text-amber-700 leading-relaxed">Ziel auf die Untergrenze {plan.floor} kcal angehoben — schneller abzunehmen würde Training & Gesundheit untergraben.</div>}
          {plan.calibrated && <button onClick={() => set("tdeeManual", null)} className="text-[10px] font-semibold text-slate-400 underline">Kalibrierung zurücksetzen (zurück zur Formel)</button>}
        </div>
      ) : <div className="rounded-xl bg-slate-100 p-3 text-[11px] text-slate-500">Alter, Größe und Gewicht eintragen — dann erscheint hier dein berechnetes Tagesziel.</div>}
      <button onClick={() => plan && onSave(f)} disabled={!plan} className="w-full rounded-xl bg-indigo-600 text-white py-2.5 text-sm font-semibold disabled:opacity-40">{submitLabel}</button>
    </div>
  );
}
function NutritionTab({ data, setData, plan }) {
  const dark = useDark();
  const nut = { ...NUT_DEFAULT, ...(data.nutrition || {}), profile: { ...NUT_DEFAULT.profile, ...((data.nutrition || {}).profile || {}) } };
  const kplan = kcalPlan(nut.profile);
  const saveProfile = (profile) => setData((d) => {
    const cur = { ...NUT_DEFAULT, ...(d.nutrition || {}) };
    const seed = (!cur.weightLog || !cur.weightLog.length) && parseNum(profile.weight) ? [{ id: uid(), date: todayISO(), kg: parseNum(profile.weight) }] : [];
    return { ...d, nutrition: { ...cur, profile, setup: true, weightLog: [...(cur.weightLog || []), ...seed] } };
  });

  const [entry, setEntry] = useState({ date: todayISO(), kcal: "", label: "", kind: "in", tag: "", savePreset: false });
  const [editPresets, setEditPresets] = useState(false);
  const [showProfile, setShowProfile] = useState(false);
  const [wInput, setWInput] = useState("");
  const [undoN, setUndoN] = useState(null);
  const undoTimer = useRef(null);
  const pushUndo = (label, restore) => { setUndoN({ label, restore }); clearTimeout(undoTimer.current); undoTimer.current = setTimeout(() => setUndoN(null), 6000); };

  const sums = (d) => {
    const es = nut.intake.filter((e) => e.date === d);
    const inn = es.filter((e) => e.kind !== "out").reduce((s, e) => s + e.kcal, 0);
    const outM = es.filter((e) => e.kind === "out").reduce((s, e) => s + e.kcal, 0);
    const outG = garminKcalOn(data.runLog, d);
    return { inn, out: outM + outG, outG };
  };
  const targetOn = (d) => (kplan ? Math.round(kplan.target + (parseNum(nut.profile.addBack) / 100) * sums(d).out) : 0);

  if (!nut.setup || !kplan) return (
    <div className="space-y-4">
      <Card className="p-4">
        <Eyebrow color="#0d9488">Ernährung einrichten</Eyebrow>
        <p className="text-xs text-slate-500 leading-relaxed mt-1.5">Nur Kalorien, kein Lebensmittel-Tracking: Du schätzt kcal pro Mahlzeit, die App rechnet Ziel, Training und Trend. <b>Konsistent grob schlägt selten genau</b> — Schätzwerte reichen völlig.</p>
      </Card>
      <Card className="p-4"><NutritionProfileForm initial={nut.profile} onSave={saveProfile} submitLabel="Plan berechnen & starten" /></Card>
    </div>
  );

  const t = todayISO();
  const ts = sums(t);
  const targetToday = targetOn(t);
  const rest = targetToday - ts.inn;
  const pct = targetToday ? ts.inn / targetToday : 0;
  const barColor = pct > 1.07 ? "#d97706" : pct >= 0.9 ? "#0d9488" : "#6366f1";
  const todayKey = DAYS[(new Date().getDay() + 6) % 7];
  const todayLoad = plan.find((dd) => dd.day === todayKey)?.load || 0;

  const addEntry = () => {
    const k = Math.round(parseNum(entry.kcal)); if (!k) return;
    const e = { id: uid(), date: entry.date, kcal: k, kind: entry.kind, label: (entry.label || entry.tag || (entry.kind === "out" ? "Aktivität" : "Essen")).trim() };
    setData((d) => { const cur = d.nutrition; const presets = entry.savePreset ? [...cur.presets.filter((p) => !(p.label === e.label && p.kind === e.kind)), { id: uid(), label: e.label, kcal: k, kind: e.kind }].slice(-12) : cur.presets; return { ...d, nutrition: { ...cur, intake: [...cur.intake, e], presets } }; });
    setEntry((en) => ({ ...en, kcal: "", label: "", savePreset: false }));
  };
  const removeEntry = (id) => { const it = nut.intake.find((x) => x.id === id); setData((d) => ({ ...d, nutrition: { ...d.nutrition, intake: d.nutrition.intake.filter((x) => x.id !== id) } })); if (it) pushUndo("Eintrag", () => setData((d) => ({ ...d, nutrition: { ...d.nutrition, intake: [...d.nutrition.intake, it] } }))); };
  const removePreset = (id) => setData((d) => ({ ...d, nutrition: { ...d.nutrition, presets: d.nutrition.presets.filter((p) => p.id !== id) } }));
  const addWeight = () => { const kg = parseNum(wInput); if (!kg) return; setData((d) => ({ ...d, nutrition: { ...d.nutrition, weightLog: [...d.nutrition.weightLog.filter((w) => w.date !== t), { id: uid(), date: t, kg }], profile: { ...d.nutrition.profile, weight: String(kg) } } })); setWInput(""); };
  const removeWeight = (id) => { const it = nut.weightLog.find((x) => x.id === id); setData((d) => ({ ...d, nutrition: { ...d.nutrition, weightLog: d.nutrition.weightLog.filter((x) => x.id !== id) } })); if (it) pushUndo("Wiegung", () => setData((d) => ({ ...d, nutrition: { ...d.nutrition, weightLog: [...d.nutrition.weightLog, it] } }))); };

  const dayEntries = nut.intake.filter((e) => e.date === entry.date);
  const [kcalRange, setKcalRange] = useState("d14"); // kalendertag-basiert: Default entspricht bisherigem "Letzte 14 Tage"
  const kcalDayCount = { d14: 14, d30: 30, d90: 90 }[kcalRange] || 14;
  const days14 = lastNDates(kcalDayCount).map((d) => { const s = sums(d); return { date: fmtISOshort(d), in: s.inn, target: targetOn(d) }; });
  let streakN = 0; { let d = t; if (!sums(d).inn) d = isoAddDays(d, -1); while (sums(d).inn > 0) { streakN++; d = isoAddDays(d, -1); } }
  const last7 = lastNDates(7);
  const hit7 = last7.filter((d) => { const s = sums(d); if (!s.inn) return false; const tg = targetOn(d); return Math.abs(s.inn - tg) <= 0.1 * tg; }).length;
  const logged7 = last7.map((d) => sums(d).inn).filter((v) => v > 0);
  const avg7 = logged7.length ? Math.round(logged7.reduce((a, b) => a + b, 0) / logged7.length) : null;
  const now = new Date(); const mo = new Date(now); mo.setDate(now.getDate() - ((now.getDay() + 6) % 7));
  const weekIso = Array.from({ length: 7 }, (_, i) => { const d = new Date(mo); d.setDate(mo.getDate() + i); return `${d.getFullYear()}-${String(d.getMonth() + 1).padStart(2, "0")}-${String(d.getDate()).padStart(2, "0")}`; });
  const weekBudget = weekIso.reduce((s, d) => s + (d <= t ? targetOn(d) : kplan.target), 0) - weekIso.reduce((s, d) => s + sums(d).inn, 0);
  const wSorted = [...nut.weightLog].sort((a, b) => a.date.localeCompare(b.date));
  const wMa = ma7w(wSorted);
  const [weightRange, setWeightRange] = useState("d30"); // Default entspricht dem bisherigen slice(-30)
  const wChart = applyTimeRange(wMa.map((w) => ({ iso: w.date, date: fmtISOshort(w.date), kg: w.kg, ma: w.ma })), weightRange);
  let wTrend = null;
  if (wMa.length >= 2) { const span = (new Date(wMa[wMa.length - 1].date) - new Date(wMa[0].date)) / DAY_MS; if (span >= 8) wTrend = Math.round(((wMa[wMa.length - 1].ma - wMa[0].ma) / span) * 7 * 100) / 100; }
  // Realitäts-Check: echten Tagesverbrauch aus Essen + Gewichtsverlauf schätzen (21-Tage-Fenster)
  const win21 = lastNDates(21);
  const logDays = win21.filter((d) => sums(d).inn > 0);
  const wIn = wSorted.filter((w) => w.date >= win21[0]);
  let reality = null;
  if (logDays.length >= 12 && wIn.length >= 5) {
    const span = (new Date(wIn[wIn.length - 1].date) - new Date(wIn[0].date)) / DAY_MS;
    if (span >= 14) {
      const avgIn = Math.round(win21.reduce((s, d) => s + sums(d).inn, 0) / logDays.length);
      const maW = ma7w(wIn); const dKg = maW[maW.length - 1].ma - maW[0].ma;
      const est = Math.round(avgIn - (dKg * 7700) / span);
      if (est >= 1200 && est <= 6000) reality = { est, avgIn, dKg: Math.round(dKg * 10) / 10, span: Math.round(span), days: logDays.length };
    }
  }
  const need = reality ? null : { days: Math.max(0, 12 - logDays.length), weighs: Math.max(0, 5 - wIn.length) };
  const applyTdee = () => reality && setData((d) => ({ ...d, nutrition: { ...d.nutrition, profile: { ...d.nutrition.profile, tdeeManual: reality.est } } }));

  return (
    <div className="space-y-4">
      <Card className="p-4" style={{ background: barColor + (dark ? "21" : "12"), borderColor: barColor + "55" }}>
        <div className="flex items-center justify-between"><Eyebrow color={barColor}>Heute</Eyebrow><span className="text-[10px] text-slate-400 font-num">Ziel {targetToday} kcal</span></div>
        <div className="mt-1 flex items-baseline gap-2">
          <span className="font-num text-3xl font-bold" style={{ color: safeText(dark, barColor) }}>{Math.abs(rest)}</span>
          <span className="text-xs font-semibold" style={{ color: safeText(dark, barColor) }}>{rest >= 0 ? "kcal frei" : "kcal drüber"}</span>
        </div>
        <div className="mt-2 h-2 rounded-full overflow-hidden" style={{ background: dark ? "#26334a" : "#e2e8f0" }}><div className="h-full rounded-full transition-all" style={{ width: `${Math.min(100, Math.round(pct * 100))}%`, background: barColor }} /></div>
        <div className="mt-1.5 text-[10.5px] text-slate-500 font-num">Gegessen {ts.inn} · Training +{Math.round((parseNum(nut.profile.addBack) / 100) * ts.out)} angerechnet{ts.outG ? ` (Garmin ${ts.outG})` : ""}</div>
        {kplan.belowFloor && <div className="text-[10.5px] text-amber-700 mt-1">Ziel liegt auf der Gesundheits-Untergrenze ({kplan.floor} kcal).</div>}
        {nut.profile.goal === "cut" && todayLoad >= 8 && <div className="text-[10.5px] text-amber-700 mt-1">Heute ⚡{todayLoad} geplant — an harten Tagen lieber am oberen Rand essen, sonst leidet die Einheit.</div>}
      </Card>

      <Card className="p-4">
        <Eyebrow>Eintragen</Eyebrow>
        <div className="mt-2 flex gap-1.5">
          {[["in", "🍽️ Gegessen"], ["out", "🔥 Verbraucht"]].map(([v, l]) => (
