            <button key={v} onClick={() => setEntry({ ...entry, kind: v, tag: "" })} className={`flex-1 rounded-xl py-2 text-[11px] font-semibold border transition ${entry.kind === v ? "bg-slate-900 text-white border-transparent" : "bg-white text-slate-600 border-slate-200"}`}>{l}</button>
          ))}
        </div>
        {nut.presets.filter((p) => p.kind === entry.kind).length > 0 && (
          <div className="mt-2 flex flex-wrap gap-1.5 items-center">
            {nut.presets.filter((p) => p.kind === entry.kind).map((p) => (
              <span key={p.id} className="inline-flex items-center gap-1">
                <button onClick={() => setEntry({ ...entry, kcal: String(p.kcal), label: p.label })} className="rounded-full bg-slate-100 px-2.5 py-1 text-[10.5px] font-semibold text-slate-600 font-num">{p.label} · {p.kcal}</button>
                {editPresets && <button onClick={() => removePreset(p.id)} className="text-rose-500 text-[11px] font-bold px-0.5">✕</button>}
              </span>
            ))}
            <button onClick={() => setEditPresets((e) => !e)} className="text-[10px] font-semibold text-slate-400 underline">{editPresets ? "fertig" : "bearbeiten"}</button>
          </div>
        )}
        {entry.kind === "in" && <div className="mt-2 flex flex-wrap gap-1.5">{MEAL_TAGS.map((tg) => <button key={tg} onClick={() => setEntry({ ...entry, tag: entry.tag === tg ? "" : tg })} className={`rounded-full px-2.5 py-1 text-[10.5px] font-semibold border ${entry.tag === tg ? "bg-teal-600 text-white border-transparent" : "bg-white text-slate-600 border-slate-200"}`}>{tg}</button>)}</div>}
        <div className="mt-2 grid grid-cols-3 gap-2">
          <input type="date" value={entry.date} onChange={(e) => setEntry({ ...entry, date: e.target.value })} className="tc-input font-num" />
          <input inputMode="numeric" placeholder="kcal" value={entry.kcal} onChange={(e) => setEntry({ ...entry, kcal: e.target.value })} className="tc-input font-num" />
          <input placeholder="Was? (optional)" value={entry.label} onChange={(e) => setEntry({ ...entry, label: e.target.value })} className="tc-input" />
        </div>
        <label className="mt-2 flex items-center gap-2 text-[11px] text-slate-500"><input type="checkbox" checked={entry.savePreset} onChange={(e) => setEntry({ ...entry, savePreset: e.target.checked })} /> Als Schnellwahl speichern (z. B. „Schulmensa“)</label>
        <button onClick={addEntry} className="mt-2.5 w-full rounded-xl bg-teal-600 text-white py-2.5 text-sm font-semibold flex items-center justify-center gap-1.5"><Plus size={16} /> Eintragen</button>
        {dayEntries.length > 0 && (
          <div className="mt-3 divide-y divide-slate-100 border-t border-slate-200/70">
            {dayEntries.map((e) => (
              <div key={e.id} className="flex items-center gap-2.5 py-2">
                <span className="text-xs text-slate-700 flex-1 truncate">{e.label}</span>
                <span className={`font-num text-sm font-semibold shrink-0 ${e.kind === "out" ? "text-amber-700" : "text-slate-800"}`}>{e.kind === "out" ? "−" : "+"}{e.kcal}</span>
                <button onClick={() => removeEntry(e.id)} className="text-slate-300 shrink-0"><Trash2 size={14} /></button>
              </div>
            ))}
          </div>
        )}
      </Card>

      <Card className="p-4">
        <div className="flex items-center justify-between"><Eyebrow>Kalorien-Verlauf</Eyebrow><TimeRangeSelect value={kcalRange} onChange={setKcalRange} only={["d14", "d30", "d90"]} /></div>
        <div style={{ width: "100%", height: 150 }} className="mt-1"><ResponsiveContainer>
          <ComposedChart data={days14} margin={{ top: 5, right: 8, left: -4, bottom: 0 }}>
            <CartesianGrid strokeDasharray="3 3" stroke={gridCol(dark)} vertical={false} />
            <XAxis dataKey="date" tick={{ fontSize: 9, fill: "#94a3b8" }} interval="preserveStartEnd" />
            <YAxis tick={{ fontSize: 10, fill: "#94a3b8" }} width={40} />
            <Tooltip formatter={(v, name) => [v + " kcal", name === "in" ? "Gegessen" : "Tagesziel"]} {...tipTop(dark)} />
            <Bar dataKey="in" fill="#6366f1" radius={[3, 3, 0, 0]} maxBarSize={16} />
            <Line type="stepAfter" dataKey="target" stroke={dark ? "#e2e8f0" : "#0f172a"} strokeWidth={1.5} strokeDasharray="4 3" dot={false} />
          </ComposedChart>
        </ResponsiveContainer></div>
        <div className="mt-2 flex gap-2.5">
          <Stat label="Streak" value={streakN} unit="Tage" accent="#f59e0b" icon={<Flame size={13} className="text-amber-500" />} />
          <Stat label="Ø 7 Tage" value={avg7 || "—"} unit={avg7 ? "kcal" : ""} accent="#6366f1" icon={<Utensils size={13} className="text-indigo-500" />} />
          <Stat label="Im Ziel (7T)" value={`${hit7}/7`} accent="#0d9488" icon={<Check size={13} className="text-teal-600" />} />
        </div>
        <div className="mt-2 text-[10.5px] text-slate-500 font-num">Wochenbudget (Mo–So): {weekBudget >= 0 ? `noch ${weekBudget} kcal frei` : `${-weekBudget} kcal über Budget`}</div>
        <div className="mt-2"><InfoToggle label="Wie zählt das Training?">Kalorien deiner Garmin-Läufe fließen am jeweiligen Tag automatisch als Verbrauch ein; Volleyball/Kraft kannst du oben als „Verbraucht“ schätzen. Angerechnet werden {parseNum(nut.profile.addBack)} % davon (im Profil änderbar) — 50 % ist der bewährte Mittelweg, weil Uhren-Kalorien oft zu hoch schätzen.</InfoToggle></div>
      </Card>

      <Card className="p-4">
        <div className="flex items-baseline justify-between gap-1.5 flex-wrap">
          <Eyebrow color="#0d9488">Gewicht</Eyebrow>
          <div className="flex items-center gap-1.5">
            {wTrend != null && <span className="text-[10.5px] font-num text-slate-500">{wTrend > 0 ? "+" : ""}{wTrend} kg/Woche (Trend)</span>}
            <TimeRangeSelect value={weightRange} onChange={setWeightRange} />
          </div>
        </div>
        <div className="mt-2 flex gap-2">
          <input inputMode="decimal" placeholder="heute (kg)" value={wInput} onChange={(e) => setWInput(e.target.value)} className="tc-input font-num" />
          <button onClick={addWeight} className="h-11 w-11 rounded-xl bg-teal-600 text-white flex items-center justify-center shrink-0"><Plus size={16} /></button>
        </div>
        {wChart.length >= 2 ? (
          <div style={{ width: "100%", height: 140 }} className="mt-2"><ResponsiveContainer>
            <LineChart data={wChart} margin={{ top: 5, right: 8, left: -4, bottom: 0 }}>
              <CartesianGrid strokeDasharray="3 3" stroke={gridCol(dark)} />
              <XAxis dataKey="date" tick={{ fontSize: 9, fill: "#94a3b8" }} interval="preserveStartEnd" />
              <YAxis domain={["dataMin - 1", "dataMax + 1"]} tick={{ fontSize: 10, fill: "#94a3b8" }} width={38} tickFormatter={(v) => v.toFixed(1)} />
              <Tooltip formatter={(v, name) => [v + " kg", name === "ma" ? "7-Tage-Schnitt" : "Wiegung"]} {...tipTop(dark)} />
              {parseNum(nut.profile.goalWeight) > 0 && <ReferenceLine y={parseNum(nut.profile.goalWeight)} stroke="#0d9488" strokeDasharray="4 4" label={chipLabel("Ziel", "#0d9488", dark, chipSide(wChart.map((p) => p.kg), parseNum(nut.profile.goalWeight), Math.max(...wChart.map((p) => p.kg)) - Math.min(...wChart.map((p) => p.kg)) + 2, "below"))} />}
              <Line type="linear" dataKey="kg" stroke={dark ? "#818cf8" : "#a5b4fc"} strokeWidth={1} dot={{ r: 2 }} />
              <Line type="linear" dataKey="ma" stroke="#0d9488" strokeWidth={2.5} dot={false} />
            </LineChart>
          </ResponsiveContainer></div>
        ) : <div className="py-4 text-center text-xs text-slate-400 mt-1">{wMa.length >= 2 ? "Zu wenig Wiegungen in diesem Zeitraum." : "Ab 2 Wiegungen erscheint hier dein Verlauf mit 7-Tage-Schnitt — die Tageszahl schwankt, der Schnitt zählt."}</div>}
        {wSorted.length > 0 && (
          <div className="mt-2 flex flex-wrap gap-1.5">{[...wSorted].slice(-4).reverse().map((w) => <span key={w.id} className="inline-flex items-center gap-1 rounded-full bg-slate-100 px-2 py-0.5 text-[10.5px] font-num text-slate-600">{fmtISOshort(w.date)} · {w.kg} kg <button onClick={() => removeWeight(w.id)} className="text-slate-300"><Trash2 size={11} /></button></span>)}</div>
        )}
      </Card>

      <Card className="p-4">
        <Eyebrow color="#7c3aed">Realitäts-Check (echter Verbrauch)</Eyebrow>
        {reality ? (
          <>
            <div className="mt-1.5 flex items-baseline gap-2"><span className="font-num text-2xl font-bold text-slate-900">{reality.est}</span><span className="text-[11px] text-slate-500">kcal/Tag tatsächlich verbraucht</span></div>
            <div className="text-[10.5px] text-slate-500 mt-1 font-num leading-relaxed">Aus Ø {reality.avgIn} kcal gegessen und {reality.dKg > 0 ? "+" : ""}{reality.dKg} kg über {reality.span} Tage ({reality.days} Log-Tage). Formel-Annahme aktuell: {kplan.tdee} kcal.</div>
            {Math.abs(reality.est - kplan.tdee) < 80
              ? <div className="text-[10.5px] text-teal-700 mt-1.5">Passt — deine Formel-Annahme trifft die Realität, nichts anzupassen.</div>
              : <button onClick={applyTdee} className="mt-2 w-full rounded-xl bg-violet-600 text-white py-2.5 text-xs font-semibold">Als Verbrauch übernehmen → neues Tagesziel</button>}
          </>
        ) : (
          <div className="text-xs text-slate-500 mt-1.5 leading-relaxed">Der stärkste Trick guter Ernährungs-Apps: aus Essen + Gewichtsverlauf deinen <b>echten</b> Verbrauch berechnen, statt der Formel blind zu glauben. Noch nötig: <b>{need.days} Log-Tage</b> und <b>{need.weighs} Wiegungen</b> (im 21-Tage-Fenster, erste und letzte Wiegung mind. 14 Tage auseinander).</div>
        )}
        <div className="mt-2"><InfoToggle label="Wie wird gerechnet?">Ø-Kalorienaufnahme minus Gewichtsänderung × 7700 kcal/kg über den Zeitraum. Nur aussagekräftig, wenn (fast) jeder Tag geloggt ist — Lücken verfälschen das Ergebnis nach unten.</InfoToggle></div>
      </Card>

      <Card className="p-4">
        <button onClick={() => setShowProfile((s) => !s)} className="w-full flex items-center justify-between text-left">
          <Eyebrow>Profil & Ziel</Eyebrow>
          <ChevronDown size={15} className={`text-slate-400 transition-transform ${showProfile ? "rotate-180" : ""}`} />
        </button>
        {showProfile && <div className="mt-3"><NutritionProfileForm initial={nut.profile} onSave={(p) => { saveProfile(p); setShowProfile(false); }} submitLabel="Speichern" /></div>}
      </Card>

      <UndoToast undo={undoN} onUndo={() => { if (undoN) undoN.restore(); setUndoN(null); }} />
    </div>
  );
}

/* ===================== V3/v7.0: GARMIN — Workout-Rezept für die Uhr =====================
   v7.0: Der experimentelle .FIT-Datei-Export ist bewusst entfernt (Nutzer-Feedback: praktisch nicht
   nutzbar; der Hardware-Test kam nie zustande). Das Rezept + Garmin-Connect-Weg bleibt — die interne
   Schritt-Struktur (WKT/hrTgt/paceTgt) beschreibt weiterhin die Einheit und speist die Rezept-Zeilen. */
const WKT = { DUR_TIME: 0, DUR_DIST: 1, DUR_OPEN: 5, DUR_REPEAT: 6, TGT_SPEED: 0, TGT_HR: 1, TGT_OPEN: 2, INT_ACTIVE: 0, INT_REST: 1, INT_WARM: 2, INT_COOL: 3 };
const hrTgt = (lo, hi) => ({ tgt: WKT.TGT_HR, tgtVal: 0, low: lo + 100, high: hi + 100 }); // Konvention aus dem FIT-Format beibehalten: bpm = Wert − 100
const paceTgt = (paceSec, pm = 0.05) => { const v = 1000000 / paceSec; return { tgt: WKT.TGT_SPEED, tgtVal: 0, low: Math.round(v * (1 - pm)), high: Math.round(v * (1 + pm)) }; }; // Geschwindigkeit in mm/s
const OPEN_TGT = { tgt: WKT.TGT_OPEN, tgtVal: 0, low: 0, high: 0 };
const parseHrRange = (hr) => { const m = /(\d+)\s*[–-]\s*(\d+)/.exec(hr || ""); return m ? [+m[1], +m[2]] : null; };
const parseMinutesAvg = (s) => { const m = /(\d+)(?:\s*[–-]\s*(\d+))?\s*Min/i.exec(s || ""); return m ? Math.round((+m[1] + (+(m[2] || m[1]))) / 2) : null; };
const parseReps = (s) => { const m = /(\d+)\s*[×x]\s*(\d+(?:[.,]\d+)?)\s*(m|km)\b/i.exec(s || ""); if (!m) return null; const d = parseFloat(m[2].replace(",", ".")); return { n: +m[1], distM: Math.round(m[3].toLowerCase() === "km" ? d * 1000 : d) }; };
const parsePauseSec = (s) => { const m = /(\d+(?:[.,]\d+)?)\s*Min\s*Pause/i.exec(s || ""); if (m) return Math.round(parseFloat(m[1].replace(",", ".")) * 60); const m2 = /(\d+)\s*s(?:ek)?\w*\s*Pause/i.exec(s || ""); return m2 ? +m2[1] : 120; };
// Plan-Session → strukturiertes Garmin-Workout (HF-/Pace-Zielbereiche & Wiederholungen voreingestellt)
function buildGarminWorkout(item, week) {
  const hr = parseHrRange(item.hr);
  const warm = { name: "Aufwärmen", int: WKT.INT_WARM, dur: WKT.DUR_TIME, durVal: 10 * 60 * 1000, ...OPEN_TGT };
  const cool = { name: "Auslaufen", int: WKT.INT_COOL, dur: WKT.DUR_TIME, durVal: 5 * 60 * 1000, ...OPEN_TGT };
  const short = { easy: "Easy", tempo: "Tempo", int: "Intervalle", long: "Lang", test: "5K-Test" }[item.type];
  if (!short) return null;
  const name = `W${week} ${short}`;
  let steps = [];
  if (item.type === "easy" || item.type === "long") {
    const min = parseMinutesAvg(item.dur) || 30;
    steps = [{ name: short, int: WKT.INT_ACTIVE, dur: WKT.DUR_TIME, durVal: min * 60 * 1000, ...(hr ? hrTgt(hr[0], hr[1]) : OPEN_TGT) }];
  } else if (item.type === "tempo") {
    const min = parseMinutesAvg(item.dur) || 20;
    steps = [warm, { name: "Tempo", int: WKT.INT_ACTIVE, dur: WKT.DUR_TIME, durVal: min * 60 * 1000, ...(hr ? hrTgt(hr[0], hr[1]) : paceTgt(targetPaceSec("tempo", week))) }, cool];
  } else if (item.type === "int") {
    const reps = parseReps(item.dur) || parseReps(item.desc) || { n: 5, distM: 800 };
    const pause = parsePauseSec(item.desc || item.dur);
    steps = [warm,
      { name: `${reps.distM} m`, int: WKT.INT_ACTIVE, dur: WKT.DUR_DIST, durVal: reps.distM * 100, ...paceTgt(targetPaceSec("int", week)) },
      { name: "Trabpause", int: WKT.INT_REST, dur: WKT.DUR_TIME, durVal: pause * 1000, ...OPEN_TGT },
      { name: "Wiederholen", int: WKT.INT_ACTIVE, dur: WKT.DUR_REPEAT, durVal: 1, tgt: WKT.TGT_OPEN, tgtVal: reps.n, low: 0, high: 0 },
      cool];
  } else if (item.type === "test") {
    steps = [warm, { name: "5 km Bestzeit", int: WKT.INT_ACTIVE, dur: WKT.DUR_DIST, durVal: 500000, ...OPEN_TGT }, cool];
  }
  return { name, steps };
}
function workoutRecipeLines(spec) {
  return spec.steps.map((s, idx) => {
    const n = idx + 1;
    if (s.dur === WKT.DUR_REPEAT) return `${n}. Wiederholen: Schritte ${s.durVal + 1}–${idx} ×${s.tgtVal}`;
    const d = (s.durVal || 0) / 100;
    const dur = s.dur === WKT.DUR_TIME ? `${Math.round(s.durVal / 60000)} Min` : s.dur === WKT.DUR_DIST ? (d >= 1000 ? `${d / 1000} km` : `${d} m`) : "offen";
    const tgt = s.tgt === WKT.TGT_HR ? `HF ${s.low - 100}–${s.high - 100}` : s.tgt === WKT.TGT_SPEED ? `Pace ${secToMMSS(Math.round(1000000 / s.high))}–${secToMMSS(Math.round(1000000 / s.low))}/km` : "locker";
    return `${n}. ${s.name} — ${dur}, ${tgt}`;
  });
}
function GarminExport({ item, week }) {
  const spec = useMemo(() => buildGarminWorkout(item, week), [item, week]);
  const [copied, setCopied] = useState(false);
  if (!spec) return null;
  const lines = workoutRecipeLines(spec);
  const copy = async () => { try { await navigator.clipboard.writeText(spec.name + "\n" + lines.join("\n")); setCopied(true); setTimeout(() => setCopied(false), 2000); } catch (_) {} };
  return (
    <div className="rounded-xl bg-slate-100 p-2.5 space-y-2">
      <div className="flex items-center gap-1.5 text-[10px] font-semibold text-slate-500"><Watch size={12} /> Auf die Garmin-Uhr</div>
      <ul className="space-y-0.5">{lines.map((l, i) => <li key={i} className="text-[10.5px] text-slate-600 font-num">{l}</li>)}</ul>
      <button onClick={copy} className="w-full rounded-lg bg-white border border-slate-200 text-slate-700 py-2 text-[11px] font-semibold inline-flex items-center justify-center gap-1"><Copy size={12} /> {copied ? "Kopiert ✓" : "Rezept kopieren"}</button>
      <InfoToggle label="So kommt's auf die Forerunner 55">
        „Rezept kopieren“ und in der Garmin-Connect-App unter Mehr → Training → Trainings 1:1 anlegen — synchronisiert automatisch auf die Uhr. HF-/Pace-Zielbereiche, Distanzen und Wiederholungen stehen oben fertig aufgelistet; einmal pro Blockwechsel anlegen reicht (die Einheiten ändern sich nur zwischen den Blöcken).
      </InfoToggle>
    </div>
  );
}

/* ===================== EINSTELLUNGEN ===================== */
function ThemeCard({ data, setData }) {
  const theme = data.theme || "auto";
  const opts = [["light", "Hell", Sun], ["dark", "Dunkel", Moon], ["auto", "Auto", MonitorSmartphone]];
  return (
    <Card className="p-4">
      <Eyebrow>Darstellung</Eyebrow>
      <div className="mt-2.5 flex gap-2">
        {opts.map(([id, label, Icon]) => (
          <button key={id} onClick={() => setData((d) => ({ ...d, theme: id }))}
            className={`flex-1 rounded-xl py-2.5 text-xs font-semibold border transition flex flex-col items-center gap-1 ${theme === id ? "bg-indigo-600 text-white border-transparent" : "bg-white text-slate-600 border-slate-200"}`}>
            <Icon size={16} /> {label}
          </button>
        ))}
      </div>
      <div className="text-[11px] text-slate-400 mt-2">„Auto" folgt der Systemeinstellung deines Geräts.</div>
    </Card>
  );
}
function VBSlotsCard({ data, setData }) {
  const slots = data.vbSlots?.length ? data.vbSlots : DEFAULT_VB_SLOTS;
  const update = (i, field, val) => setData((d) => { const next = [...(d.vbSlots?.length ? d.vbSlots : DEFAULT_VB_SLOTS)]; next[i] = { ...next[i], [field]: val }; return { ...d, vbSlots: next }; });
  const removeSlot = (i) => setData((d) => { const next = [...(d.vbSlots?.length ? d.vbSlots : DEFAULT_VB_SLOTS)]; next.splice(i, 1); return { ...d, vbSlots: next }; });
  const addSlot = () => setData((d) => ({ ...d, vbSlots: [...(d.vbSlots?.length ? d.vbSlots : DEFAULT_VB_SLOTS), { day: "Mi", time: "19:00" }] }));
  return (
    <Card className="p-4">
      <Eyebrow>Volleyball-Trainingszeiten</Eyebrow>
      <p className="text-[11px] text-slate-400 mt-1 mb-2 leading-relaxed">Gilt für alle Wochen (z. B. wenn der Verein in den Ferien andere Zeiten hat). Turnier- und Testwochen-Sonderregeln bleiben aktiv. Pro Tag zählt der letzte Eintrag.</p>
      <div className="space-y-2">
        {slots.map((s, i) => (
          <div key={i} className="flex items-center gap-2">
            <select value={s.day} onChange={(e) => update(i, "day", e.target.value)} className="tc-input" style={{ width: 84, flexShrink: 0 }}>{DAYS.map((d) => <option key={d} value={d}>{d}</option>)}</select>
            <input type="time" value={s.time} onChange={(e) => update(i, "time", e.target.value)} className="tc-input font-num" />
            <button onClick={() => removeSlot(i)} disabled={slots.length <= 1} className="h-11 w-11 rounded-xl bg-slate-100 flex items-center justify-center text-slate-500 disabled:opacity-30 shrink-0"><Trash2 size={15} /></button>
          </div>
        ))}
      </div>
      {slots.length < 4 && <button onClick={addSlot} className="mt-2.5 w-full rounded-xl border-2 border-dashed border-slate-300 py-2.5 text-xs font-semibold text-slate-600 flex items-center justify-center gap-1.5"><Plus size={14} /> Trainingszeit hinzufügen</button>}
    </Card>
  );
}

/* ===================== SCHULE ===================== */
function SchoolTab({ data, setData }) {
  const dark = useDark();
  const [form, setForm] = useState({ titel: "", fach: "", faelligkeit: todayISO(), art: "hausaufgabe" });
  const [editingId, setEditingId] = useState(null);
  const resetForm = () => setForm((f) => ({ titel: "", fach: "", faelligkeit: todayISO(), art: f.art }));
  const save = () => {
    if (!form.titel.trim()) return;
    if (editingId) {
      setData((d) => ({ ...d, schoolLog: d.schoolLog.map((s) => (s.id === editingId ? { ...s, titel: form.titel.trim(), fach: form.fach.trim(), faelligkeit: form.faelligkeit, art: form.art } : s)) }));
      setEditingId(null);
    } else {
      const entry = { id: uid(), titel: form.titel.trim(), fach: form.fach.trim(), faelligkeit: form.faelligkeit, art: form.art, erledigt: false };
      setData((d) => ({ ...d, schoolLog: [...d.schoolLog, entry] }));
    }
    resetForm();
  };
  const startEdit = (item) => {
    setEditingId(item.id);
    setForm({ titel: item.titel, fach: item.fach, faelligkeit: item.faelligkeit, art: item.art });
  };
  const cancelEdit = () => {
    setEditingId(null);
    resetForm();
  };
  const toggleErledigt = (id) => setData((d) => ({ ...d, schoolLog: d.schoolLog.map((s) => (s.id === id ? { ...s, erledigt: !s.erledigt } : s)) }));
  const { undo, trigger: triggerUndo, doUndo } = useUndoDelete(setData);
  const remove = (id) => {
    const item = data.schoolLog.find((s) => s.id === id);
    setData((d) => ({ ...d, schoolLog: d.schoolLog.filter((s) => s.id !== id) }));
    if (item) triggerUndo(item.art === "klausur" ? "Klausur" : "Hausaufgabe", "schoolLog", item);
    if (editingId === id) cancelEdit();
  };
  const [sortMode, setSortMode] = useState("faellig"); // v6.0: "faellig" (Was ist zuerst dran?) | "fach" (gruppiert)
  const sorted = [...data.schoolLog].sort((a, b) => (a.erledigt === b.erledigt ? a.faelligkeit.localeCompare(b.faelligkeit) : a.erledigt ? 1 : -1));
  const openItems = sorted.filter((s) => !s.erledigt);
  const doneItems = sorted.filter((s) => s.erledigt);
  const openCount = openItems.length;
  const overdueCount = openItems.filter((s) => daysUntil(s.faelligkeit) < 0).length;

  return (
    <div className="space-y-4">
      <Card className="p-4">
        <Eyebrow>{editingId ? "Eintrag bearbeiten" : "Neu eintragen"}</Eyebrow>
        <div className="mt-3 space-y-2.5">
          <input placeholder="Was? (z. B. Mathe S. 42, Aufgabe 3)" value={form.titel} onChange={(e) => setForm({ ...form, titel: e.target.value })} className="tc-input" />
          <div className="grid grid-cols-2 gap-2.5">
            <div>
              <div className="text-[11px] font-semibold text-slate-500 mb-1.5">Fach (optional)</div>
              <input placeholder="z. B. Mathe" value={form.fach} onChange={(e) => setForm({ ...form, fach: e.target.value })} className="tc-input" />
            </div>
            <div>
              <div className="text-[11px] font-semibold text-slate-500 mb-1.5">Fällig bis</div>
              <input type="date" value={form.faelligkeit} onChange={(e) => setForm({ ...form, faelligkeit: e.target.value })} className="tc-input font-num" />
            </div>
          </div>
          <div className="flex gap-1.5">
            {SCHOOL_ART.map(([v, l]) => (
              <button key={v} onClick={() => setForm({ ...form, art: v })} className={`flex-1 rounded-lg px-2 py-2 text-[11px] font-semibold border transition ${form.art === v ? "bg-indigo-600 text-white border-transparent" : "bg-white text-slate-600 border-slate-200"}`}>{l}</button>
            ))}
          </div>
          <div className="flex gap-2">
            <button onClick={save} className="flex-1 rounded-xl bg-indigo-600 text-white py-2.5 text-sm font-semibold flex items-center justify-center gap-1.5">
              {editingId ? <Check size={16} /> : <Plus size={16} />} {editingId ? "Speichern" : "Eintragen"}
            </button>
            {editingId && (
              <button onClick={cancelEdit} className="rounded-xl border border-slate-200 text-slate-500 px-4 py-2.5 text-sm font-semibold">Abbrechen</button>
            )}
          </div>
        </div>
      </Card>

      <Card className="p-4">
        <div className="flex items-center justify-between mb-2">
          <Eyebrow>Einträge</Eyebrow>
          <span className="text-[11px] font-num text-slate-400">{openCount} offen{overdueCount ? ` · ${overdueCount} überfällig` : ""}</span>
        </div>
        {data.schoolLog.length > 1 && (
          <div className="flex gap-1.5 mb-2.5">
            {[["faellig", "Nach Fälligkeit"], ["fach", "Nach Fach"]].map(([v, l]) => (
              <button key={v} onClick={() => setSortMode(v)} className={`flex-1 rounded-lg px-2 py-1.5 text-[11px] font-semibold border transition ${sortMode === v ? "bg-indigo-600 text-white border-transparent" : "bg-white text-slate-600 border-slate-200"}`}>{l}</button>
            ))}
          </div>
        )}
        {(() => {
          // v6.0: Klausuren klar von Hausaufgaben abheben (rose Randbalken + Chip), Liste wahlweise nach Fach gruppiert
          const renderRow = (item) => {
            const status = schoolStatus(item);
            const [accent, bright] = RECO_COLORS[status.tone] || RECO_COLORS.none;
            const col = dark ? bright : accent;
            const base = item.id === editingId ? { borderColor: "#6366f1" } : item.erledigt ? { borderColor: dark ? "#26334a" : "#e2e8f0" } : { borderColor: col + "55", background: col + (dark ? "1a" : "10") };
            const klausurEdge = item.art === "klausur" && !item.erledigt && item.id !== editingId ? { borderLeft: `3px solid ${dark ? "#fb7185" : KLAUSUR_COLOR}` } : {};
            return (
              <div key={item.id} className="rounded-xl border p-3 flex items-center gap-3" style={{ ...base, ...klausurEdge }}>
                <button onClick={() => toggleErledigt(item.id)} className="h-8 w-8 rounded-lg border-2 flex items-center justify-center shrink-0 transition" style={{ borderColor: item.erledigt ? "#0d9488" : (dark ? "#3b4a63" : "#cbd5e1"), background: item.erledigt ? "#0d9488" : "transparent" }}>
                  {item.erledigt && <Check size={14} color="#fff" strokeWidth={3} />}
                </button>
                <div className="min-w-0 flex-1">
                  <div className={`text-sm font-semibold ${item.erledigt ? "line-through text-slate-400" : "text-slate-800"}`}>{item.titel}</div>
                  <div className="text-xs text-slate-500 flex items-center gap-1.5 flex-wrap mt-0.5">
                    {item.fach && sortMode !== "fach" && <span>{item.fach}</span>}
                    {item.art === "klausur" && <span className="inline-flex items-center gap-1 rounded px-1.5 py-0.5 text-[10px] font-semibold bg-rose-100 text-rose-700"><GraduationCap size={10} /> Klausur</span>}
                    {!item.erledigt && <span className="font-semibold" style={{ color: col }}>{status.label}</span>}
                  </div>
                </div>
                <button onClick={() => startEdit(item)} className="shrink-0 p-1.5 text-slate-300"><Pencil size={15} /></button>
                <button onClick={() => remove(item.id)} className="shrink-0 p-1.5 text-slate-300"><Trash2 size={15} /></button>
              </div>
            );
          };
          if (!sorted.length) return <div className="py-8 text-center text-xs text-slate-400">Noch nichts eingetragen.</div>;
          if (sortMode !== "fach") return <div className="space-y-2">{sorted.map(renderRow)}</div>;
          return (
            <div className="space-y-3.5">
              {groupByFach(openItems).map((g) => (
                <div key={g.fach}>
                  <div className="text-[10px] font-bold uppercase tracking-wider text-slate-400 mb-1.5">{g.fach} <span className="font-num">· {g.items.length}</span></div>
                  <div className="space-y-2">{g.items.map(renderRow)}</div>
                </div>
              ))}
              {doneItems.length > 0 && (
                <div>
                  <div className="text-[10px] font-bold uppercase tracking-wider text-slate-400 mb-1.5">Erledigt</div>
                  <div className="space-y-2">{doneItems.map(renderRow)}</div>
                </div>
              )}
            </div>
          );
        })()}
      </Card>

      <UndoToast undo={undo} onUndo={doUndo} />
    </div>
  );
}

/* v5.0: Was passiert nach Krankheits-Wochen mit dem Plan-Ende? Nur relevant, wenn Krankheiten eingetragen sind. */
function PlanEndModeCard({ data, setData }) {
  if (!(data.illnessLog || []).length) return null;
  const lost = lostTrainingWeeks(data.illnessLog);
  const mode = data.planEndMode === "dynamic" ? "dynamic" : "fixed";
  const opts = [
    ["fixed", "Testtermin fest", "Endblock wird kürzer"],
    ["dynamic", "Test verschieben", lost ? `Plan +${lost} Woche${lost === 1 ? "" : "n"}` : "Plan verlängert sich"],
  ];
  return (
    <Card className="p-4">
      <Eyebrow>Laufplan nach Krankheit</Eyebrow>
      <p className="text-[11px] text-slate-400 mt-1 mb-2 leading-relaxed">Durch Krankheit verlorene Wochen verzögern die Steigerung des Laufplans automatisch. Hier entscheidest du, was das fürs Plan-Ende bedeutet.</p>
      <div className="flex gap-2">
        {opts.map(([id, label, sub]) => (
          <button key={id} onClick={() => setData((d) => ({ ...d, planEndMode: id }))}
            className={`flex-1 rounded-xl py-2.5 px-2 text-xs font-semibold border transition flex flex-col items-center gap-0.5 ${mode === id ? "bg-indigo-600 text-white border-transparent" : "bg-white text-slate-600 border-slate-200"}`}>
            <span>{label}</span><span className={`text-[9px] font-medium ${mode === id ? "text-indigo-200" : "text-slate-400"}`}>{sub}</span>
          </button>
        ))}
      </div>
      <div className="text-[11px] text-slate-400 mt-2 font-num">{lost ? `Aktuell ${lost} verlorene Woche${lost === 1 ? "" : "n"} · ` : ""}5-km-Test: Mi {fmtDM(testDateFor(data.illnessLog, mode))}</div>
    </Card>
  );
}
// v7.0: eingebaute Abzeichen einzeln ausblenden (z. B. eine ganze Fernziel-Stufe, die stört) —
// wirkt nur auf die Anzeige, die Berechnung läuft weiter (Wieder-Einblenden zeigt den echten Stand)
function BadgesSettingsCard({ data, setData }) {
  const dark = useDark();
  const hidden = data.hiddenBadgeIds || [];
  const toggle = (id) => setData((d) => { const h = d.hiddenBadgeIds || []; return { ...d, hiddenBadgeIds: h.includes(id) ? h.filter((x) => x !== id) : [...h, id] }; });
  const groups = ["run", "strength", "vb", "streak", "milestone"];
  return (
    <Card className="p-4">
      <Eyebrow>Auszeichnungen</Eyebrow>
      <p className="text-[11px] text-slate-400 mt-1 mb-2 leading-relaxed">Ausgeblendete Abzeichen verschwinden aus dem Cockpit (auch aus dem Zähler). Die Berechnung läuft weiter — beim Wieder-Einblenden ist der Stand korrekt.</p>
      <div className="space-y-2.5">
        {groups.map((gk) => (
          <div key={gk}>
            <div className="text-[10px] font-semibold uppercase tracking-wider mb-1" style={{ color: safeText(dark, BADGE_GROUPS[gk].color) }}>{BADGE_GROUPS[gk].label}</div>
            <div className="flex flex-wrap gap-1.5">
              {BADGE_CATALOG.filter((b) => b.group === gk).map((b) => {
                const off = hidden.includes(b.id);
                return (
                  <button key={b.id} onClick={() => toggle(b.id)}
                    className={`rounded-full px-2.5 py-1 text-[10.5px] font-semibold border transition ${off ? "bg-white text-slate-300 border-slate-200 line-through" : "border-transparent"}`}
                    style={off ? {} : { background: softBg(dark, BADGE_GROUPS[gk].color, BADGE_GROUPS[gk].color + "1f"), color: safeText(dark, BADGE_GROUPS[gk].color) }}>
                    {b.title}
                  </button>
                );
              })}
            </div>
          </div>
        ))}
      </div>
    </Card>
  );
}
function SettingsView({ data, setData, savedAt, onRefresh, refreshing, onReset, onClose }) {
  return (
    <div className="space-y-4">
      <Card className="p-3 flex items-center gap-3">
        <button onClick={onClose} className="h-11 w-11 rounded-xl bg-slate-100 flex items-center justify-center text-slate-600"><ChevronLeft size={18} /></button>
        <div>
          <div className="font-display font-bold text-slate-900">Einstellungen</div>
          <div className="text-[11px] text-slate-500">Darstellung · Trainingszeiten · Daten</div>
        </div>
      </Card>
      <ThemeCard data={data} setData={setData} />
      <VBSlotsCard data={data} setData={setData} />
      <PlanEndModeCard data={data} setData={setData} />
      <BadgesSettingsCard data={data} setData={setData} />
      <SyncCard data={data} setData={setData} savedAt={savedAt} onRefresh={onRefresh} refreshing={refreshing} />
      <Card className="p-4">
        <Eyebrow color="#e11d48">Daten zurücksetzen</Eyebrow>
        <p className="text-[11px] text-slate-400 mt-1 mb-2.5">Löscht alle Läufe, Kraftwerte, Check-ins, Häkchen und Einstellungen unwiderruflich.</p>
        <button onClick={onReset} className="w-full rounded-xl border border-rose-200 text-rose-600 py-2.5 text-xs font-semibold flex items-center justify-center gap-1.5"><RotateCcw size={13} /> Alles zurücksetzen</button>
      </Card>
    </div>
  );
}

/* ===================== v6.0: KALENDER (Rückkehr aus v4.2, an v5.x-Logik angepasst) =====================
   Reine Lese-Ansicht: Monat / Woche / Tag. Training kommt live aus buildWeekPlan (inkl. Krankheits-Verzug,
   Ausfällen und Ersatz-Einheiten), Schule aus schoolLog (fällig am jeweiligen Tag). Kein setData. */
function CalRow({ color, label, sub, done, cancelled, big }) {
  const dark = useDark();
  return (
    <div className="flex items-center gap-2.5" style={cancelled ? { opacity: 0.55 } : undefined}>
      <span className="h-2.5 w-2.5 rounded-full shrink-0" style={{ background: done ? (dark ? "#3b4a63" : "#cbd5e1") : color }} />
      <div className="min-w-0 flex-1">
        <div className={`${big ? "text-sm" : "text-xs"} font-semibold truncate ${done || cancelled ? "line-through text-slate-400" : "text-slate-800"}`}>{label}</div>
        {sub && <div className="text-[11px] text-slate-500 truncate">{sub}</div>}
      </div>
      {done && <Check size={14} className="text-slate-400 shrink-0" />}
    </div>
  );
}
function CalLegend() {
  return (
    <div className="mt-3 flex flex-wrap items-center gap-x-2.5 gap-y-1 text-[10px] text-slate-500">
      {["run", "vb", "strength"].map((s) => <span key={s} className="inline-flex items-center gap-1"><span className="h-2 w-2 rounded-full" style={{ background: SPORT[s].color }} /> {SPORT[s].label}</span>)}
      <span className="inline-flex items-center gap-1"><span className="h-2 w-2 rounded-full" style={{ background: CAL_SCHOOL }} /> Schule</span>
      <span className="inline-flex items-center gap-1"><span className="h-2 w-2 rounded-full" style={{ background: KLAUSUR_COLOR }} /> Klausur</span>
    </div>
  );
}
const CAL_VIEWS = [["monat", "Monat"], ["woche", "Woche"], ["tag", "Tag"]];
function CalendarTab({ data }) {
  const dark = useDark();
  const [view, setView] = useState("monat");
  const [anchor, setAnchor] = useState(() => atMidnight(new Date()));
  const [filter, setFilter] = useState({ training: true, schule: true });
  const todayIso = toLocalISO(new Date());
  const days = useMemo(() => (view === "monat" ? monthGrid(anchor) : view === "woche" ? weekGrid(anchor) : [atMidnight(anchor)]), [view, anchor]);
  const byDay = useMemo(() => {
    const cache = {};
    const getPlan = (w) => cache[w] || (cache[w] = buildWeekPlan(w, undefined, data.vbSlots, data.illnessLog, data.planEndMode, data.overrides));
    const out = {};
    for (const d of days) {
      const iso = toLocalISO(d);
      const w = rawPlanWeekOf(d, data.illnessLog, data.planEndMode);
      // Ausgefallene Einheiten (load 0) bewusst mitnehmen: der Tag soll zeigen, DASS etwas ausfiel
      const items = w ? ((getPlan(w).find((x) => x.day === DAYS[(d.getDay() + 6) % 7]) || {}).items || []).filter((it) => it.load > 0 || it.cancelled) : [];
      out[iso] = { items, school: data.schoolLog.filter((s) => s.faelligkeit === iso) };
    }
    return out;
  }, [days, data.vbSlots, data.illnessLog, data.planEndMode, data.overrides, data.schoolLog]);
  const nav = (f) => setAnchor((a) => (view === "monat" ? new Date(a.getFullYear(), a.getMonth() + f, 1) : new Date(atMidnight(a).getTime() + f * (view === "woche" ? 7 : 1) * DAY_MS)));
  const title = view === "monat" ? anchor.toLocaleDateString("de-DE", { month: "long", year: "numeric" })
    : view === "woche" ? `Woche ab ${fmtDM(mondayOf(anchor))}`
    : anchor.toLocaleDateString("de-DE", { weekday: "long", day: "2-digit", month: "2-digit" });
  const dots = (iso) => {
    const e = byDay[iso]; if (!e) return [];
    const out = [];
    if (filter.training) { const seen = new Set(); for (const it of e.items) { if (it.cancelled) continue; if (!seen.has(it.sport)) { seen.add(it.sport); out.push(SPORT[it.sport].color); } } }
    if (filter.schule && e.school.length) out.push(e.school.some((s) => s.art === "klausur" && !s.erledigt) ? KLAUSUR_COLOR : CAL_SCHOOL);
    return out.slice(0, 4);
  };
  const trainingSub = (it, big) => {
    if (it.cancelled) return "ausgefallen";
    const parts = [];
    if (it.replacement) parts.push("Ersatz");
    if (big && it.desc) parts.push(it.desc); else if (it.dur) parts.push(it.dur);
    parts.push(`⚡${it.load}`);
    if (it.illness === "sick" && !data.done[it.uid]) parts.push("entschuldigt (krank)");
    return parts.join(" · ");
  };
  const trainingRows = (e, big) => e.items.map((it) => (
    <CalRow key={it.uid} big={big} color={SPORT[it.sport].color} done={!!data.done[it.uid]} cancelled={!!it.cancelled}
      label={it.label + (it.time ? ` · ${it.time}` : "")} sub={trainingSub(it, big)} />
  ));
  const schoolRows = (e, big) => e.school.map((s) => (
    <CalRow key={s.id} big={big} color={s.art === "klausur" ? KLAUSUR_COLOR : CAL_SCHOOL} done={!!s.erledigt}
      label={s.titel} sub={[s.fach || null, s.art === "klausur" ? "Klausur" : "Hausaufgabe", big ? schoolStatus(s).label : null].filter(Boolean).join(" · ")} />
  ));
  return (
    <div className="space-y-4">
      <Card className="p-3 space-y-2.5">
        <div className="flex gap-1 rounded-2xl bg-slate-100 p-1">
          {CAL_VIEWS.map(([v, l]) => (
            <button key={v} onClick={() => setView(v)} className={`flex-1 rounded-xl py-2 text-xs font-bold transition ${view === v ? "bg-white shadow-sm text-indigo-700" : "text-slate-500"}`}>{l}</button>
          ))}
        </div>
        <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
          <button onClick={() => nav(-1)} className="h-11 w-11 rounded-xl bg-slate-100 flex items-center justify-center shrink-0" aria-label="Zurück"><ChevronLeft size={18} /></button>
          <div className="flex-1 text-center font-display font-bold text-slate-900 capitalize">{title}</div>
          <button onClick={() => nav(1)} className="h-11 w-11 rounded-xl bg-slate-100 flex items-center justify-center shrink-0" aria-label="Weiter"><ChevronRight size={18} /></button>
        </div>
        <div className="flex items-center gap-1.5">
          {[["training", "Training", "#6366f1"], ["schule", "Schule", CAL_SCHOOL]].map(([k, l, c]) => (
            <button key={k} onClick={() => setFilter((f) => ({ ...f, [k]: !f[k] }))} className={`rounded-lg px-2.5 py-1.5 text-[11px] font-semibold border transition ${filter[k] ? "text-white border-transparent" : "bg-white text-slate-400 border-slate-200"}`} style={filter[k] ? { background: c } : {}}>{l}</button>
          ))}
          <button onClick={() => { setAnchor(atMidnight(new Date())); }} className="ml-auto rounded-lg px-2.5 py-1.5 text-[11px] font-semibold border bg-white text-indigo-600 border-slate-200">Heute</button>
        </div>
      </Card>

      {view === "monat" && (
        <Card className="p-3">
          <div className="grid grid-cols-7 gap-1 mb-1">{DAYS.map((d) => <div key={d} className="text-center text-[10px] font-bold text-slate-400">{d}</div>)}</div>
          <div className="grid grid-cols-7 gap-1">
            {days.map((d) => {
              const iso = toLocalISO(d), inMonth = d.getMonth() === anchor.getMonth(), isToday = iso === todayIso;
              return (
                <button key={iso} onClick={() => { setAnchor(atMidnight(d)); setView("tag"); }}
                  className={`aspect-square rounded-lg flex flex-col items-center justify-center gap-0.5 transition ${inMonth ? "bg-slate-100" : ""}`}
                  style={{ opacity: inMonth ? 1 : 0.45, boxShadow: isToday ? "0 0 0 1.5px #6366f1" : "none" }}>
                  <span className={`text-[11px] font-num font-semibold ${isToday ? "text-indigo-600" : "text-slate-700"}`}>{d.getDate()}</span>
                  <span className="flex gap-0.5" style={{ height: 6 }}>{dots(iso).map((c, i) => <span key={i} className="rounded-full" style={{ background: c, width: 6, height: 6 }} />)}</span>
                </button>
              );
            })}
          </div>
          <CalLegend />
        </Card>
      )}

      {view === "woche" && (
        <div className="space-y-2.5">
          {days.map((d) => {
            const iso = toLocalISO(d), e = byDay[iso], isToday = iso === todayIso;
            const rows = [...(filter.training ? trainingRows(e, false) : []), ...(filter.schule ? schoolRows(e, false) : [])];
            return (
              <Card key={iso} className="p-3.5" style={isToday ? { borderColor: "#6366f1", boxShadow: "0 0 0 1px #6366f1" } : {}}>
                <div className="flex items-center gap-2 mb-1.5">
                  <span className={`text-xs font-bold ${isToday ? "text-indigo-600" : "text-slate-700"}`}>{DAY_FULL[DAYS[(d.getDay() + 6) % 7]]}</span>
                  <span className="text-[11px] text-slate-400 font-num">{fmtDM(d)}</span>
                  {isToday && <span className="text-[10px] font-semibold text-indigo-600 bg-indigo-50 rounded px-1.5 py-0.5">Heute</span>}
                </div>
                {rows.length ? <div className="space-y-1.5">{rows}</div> : <div className="text-xs text-slate-400">frei</div>}
              </Card>
            );
          })}
        </div>
      )}

      {view === "tag" && (() => {
        const iso = toLocalISO(anchor), e = byDay[iso];
        const hasAny = (filter.training && e.items.length) || (filter.schule && e.school.length);
        return (
          <Card className="p-4 space-y-3">
            {filter.training && e.items.length > 0 && <div><Eyebrow>Training</Eyebrow><div className="mt-2 space-y-2">{trainingRows(e, true)}</div></div>}
            {filter.schule && e.school.length > 0 && <div><Eyebrow color={CAL_SCHOOL}>Schule</Eyebrow><div className="mt-2 space-y-2">{schoolRows(e, true)}</div></div>}
            {!hasAny && <div className="py-6 text-center text-xs text-slate-400">Nichts an diesem Tag.</div>}
          </Card>
        );
      })()}
    </div>
  );
}

/* ===================== APP ===================== */
// Oberste Ebene: Bereiche. Training bündelt die bekannten Tabs; Kalender und Schule sind eigene Bereiche.
const AREAS = [
  { id: "training", label: "Training", icon: Dumbbell },
  { id: "kalender", label: "Kalender", icon: Calendar },
  { id: "schule", label: "Schule", icon: GraduationCap },
];
// Unter-Tabs des Trainings-Bereichs (unverändert, Cockpit ist Start)
const TABS = [
  { id: "cockpit", label: "Cockpit", icon: Gauge },
  { id: "woche", label: "Woche", icon: CalendarDays },
  { id: "kcal", label: "Kcal", icon: Utensils },
  { id: "fortschritt", label: "Fortschritt", icon: TrendingUp },
  { id: "recovery", label: "Recovery", icon: Moon },
];

export default function App() {
  const [data, setData, loaded, savedAt] = usePersistentData();
  const [area, setArea] = useState("training");
  const [tab, setTab] = useState("cockpit");
  const [showSettings, setShowSettings] = useState(false);
  const [refreshing, setRefreshing] = useState(false);
  const [sysDark, setSysDark] = useState(() => { try { return window.matchMedia?.("(prefers-color-scheme: dark)").matches || false; } catch (_) { return false; } });
  useEffect(() => {
    try {
      const mq = window.matchMedia?.("(prefers-color-scheme: dark)");
      if (!mq) return;
      const h = (e) => setSysDark(e.matches);
      mq.addEventListener?.("change", h);
      return () => mq.removeEventListener?.("change", h);
    } catch (_) {}
  }, []);
  const dark = data.theme === "dark" || (data.theme !== "light" && sysDark);

  const today = new Date();
  const currentWeek = planWeekOf(today, data.illnessLog, data.planEndMode);
  const tournamentPassed = atMidnight(today) > TOURNAMENT;
  const phaseNow = tournamentPassed ? 2 : 1;
  const daysToT = Math.ceil((TOURNAMENT - atMidnight(today)) / DAY_MS);
  const plan = useMemo(() => buildWeekPlan(currentWeek, undefined, data.vbSlots, data.illnessLog, data.planEndMode, data.overrides), [currentWeek, data.vbSlots, data.illnessLog, data.planEndMode, data.overrides]);

  const reset = () => { if (window.confirm("Alle eingetragenen Daten (Läufe, Kraftwerte, Check-ins, Häkchen) und Einstellungen löschen?")) { setData(DEFAULT_DATA); setShowSettings(false); if (hasStorage) window.storage.delete(STORAGE_KEY, false).catch(() => {}); } };
  const manualRefresh = async () => {
    if (!hasStorage) return;
    setRefreshing(true);
    try { const res = await window.storage.get(STORAGE_KEY, false); if (res?.value) { let next = { ...DEFAULT_DATA, ...JSON.parse(res.value) }; const mig = migrateDone(next.done); if (mig.changed) next = { ...next, done: mig.done }; setData(next); } } catch (_) {}
    setRefreshing(false);
  };

  // iPhone/iPad: Meta-Tags setzen, damit die App sich als Home-Bildschirm-Icon ohne Browserleiste öffnen lässt
  useEffect(() => {
    try {
      const setMeta = (name, content) => {
        let el = document.querySelector(`meta[name="${name}"]`);
        if (!el) { el = document.createElement("meta"); el.setAttribute("name", name); document.head.appendChild(el); }
        el.setAttribute("content", content);
      };
      setMeta("viewport", "width=device-width, initial-scale=1, viewport-fit=cover");
      setMeta("apple-mobile-web-app-capable", "yes");
      setMeta("mobile-web-app-capable", "yes");
      setMeta("apple-mobile-web-app-status-bar-style", "black-translucent");
      setMeta("apple-mobile-web-app-title", "Cockpit");
      setMeta("theme-color", dark ? "#0b1220" : "#0f172a");
    } catch (_) {}
  }, [dark]);

  return (
    <ThemeContext.Provider value={dark}>
    <div className={`min-h-screen tc-app bg-slate-50 ${dark ? "tc-dark" : ""}`} style={{ fontFamily: "'Plus Jakarta Sans', ui-sans-serif, system-ui, -apple-system, sans-serif" }}>
      <style>{`
        @import url('https://fonts.googleapis.com/css2?family=Plus+Jakarta+Sans:wght@400;500;600;700;800&family=Space+Grotesk:wght@500;600;700&family=JetBrains+Mono:wght@400;500;600;700&display=swap');
        .font-display{font-family:'Space Grotesk',ui-sans-serif,system-ui,sans-serif;}
        .font-num{font-family:'JetBrains Mono',ui-monospace,monospace;font-feature-settings:'tnum';}
        .tc-input{width:100%;border:1px solid #e2e8f0;border-radius:.75rem;padding:.55rem .75rem;font-size:16px;color:#0f172a;background:#fff;}
        .tc-input:focus{outline:none;border-color:#6366f1;box-shadow:0 0 0 3px rgba(99,102,241,.15);}
        @media (prefers-reduced-motion: reduce){*{transition:none!important;}}

        /* iPhone/iPad-Feinschliff */
        .tc-app{min-height:100vh;min-height:100dvh;}
        html,body{overscroll-behavior-y:contain;}
        button,a{-webkit-tap-highlight-color:transparent;touch-action:manipulation;-webkit-touch-callout:none;}
        .tc-shell{max-width:576px;}
        .tc-tablet-2col{display:block;}
        @media (min-width:768px){
          .tc-shell{max-width:720px;}
          .tc-tablet-2col{display:grid;grid-template-columns:1fr 1fr;gap:1rem;align-items:start;}
          .tc-tablet-2col > *{margin:0;}
        }
        @media (min-width:1024px){ .tc-shell{max-width:860px;} }

        /* ===== Dark-Mode (überschreibt die hellen Utility-Klassen) ===== */
        .tc-dark{color-scheme:dark;}
        .tc-dark.bg-slate-50, .tc-dark .bg-slate-50{background-color:#0b1220!important;}
        .tc-dark .bg-slate-50\\/90{background-color:rgba(11,18,32,.92)!important;}
        .tc-dark .bg-white{background-color:#141d2c!important;}
        .tc-dark .bg-white\\/60{background-color:rgba(20,29,44,.6)!important;}
        .tc-dark .bg-white\\/70{background-color:rgba(20,29,44,.75)!important;}
        .tc-dark .bg-slate-100{background-color:#1d2839!important;}
        .tc-dark .bg-indigo-50{background-color:rgba(99,102,241,.16)!important;}
        .tc-dark .bg-teal-100{background-color:rgba(13,148,136,.22)!important;}
        .tc-dark .bg-rose-100{background-color:rgba(225,29,72,.2)!important;}
        .tc-dark .bg-amber-100{background-color:rgba(245,158,11,.22)!important;}
        .tc-dark .border-slate-200, .tc-dark .border-slate-200\\/80, .tc-dark .border-slate-200\\/70{border-color:#26334a!important;}
        .tc-dark .border-slate-300{border-color:#31405c!important;}
        .tc-dark .border-indigo-300{border-color:rgba(99,102,241,.55)!important;}
        .tc-dark .border-amber-300{border-color:rgba(245,158,11,.55)!important;}
        .tc-dark .border-emerald-200{border-color:rgba(5,150,105,.5)!important;}
        .tc-dark .border-rose-200{border-color:rgba(225,29,72,.5)!important;}
        .tc-dark .divide-slate-100>:not([hidden])~:not([hidden]){border-color:#26334a!important;}
        .tc-dark .text-slate-900{color:#f1f5f9!important;}
        .tc-dark .text-slate-800{color:#e2e8f0!important;}
        .tc-dark .text-slate-700{color:#cbd5e1!important;}
        .tc-dark .text-slate-600{color:#aebccd!important;}
        .tc-dark .text-slate-500{color:#8ea0b5!important;}
        .tc-dark .text-indigo-900{color:#c7d2fe!important;}
        .tc-dark .text-indigo-700{color:#a5b4fc!important;}
        .tc-dark .text-indigo-600{color:#818cf8!important;}
        .tc-dark .text-indigo-500{color:#818cf8!important;}
        .tc-dark .text-teal-900{color:#99f6e4!important;}
        .tc-dark .text-teal-800{color:#5eead4!important;}
        .tc-dark .text-teal-700{color:#2dd4bf!important;}
        .tc-dark .text-amber-900{color:#fde68a!important;}
        .tc-dark .text-amber-800\\/80{color:rgba(252,211,77,.85)!important;}
        .tc-dark .text-amber-700{color:#fbbf24!important;}
        .tc-dark .text-emerald-900{color:#a7f3d0!important;}
        .tc-dark .text-emerald-700{color:#34d399!important;}
        .tc-dark .text-emerald-500{color:#34d399!important;}
        .tc-dark .text-rose-600{color:#fb7185!important;}
        .tc-dark .text-rose-700{color:#fda4af!important;}
        .tc-dark .text-amber-500{color:#fbbf24!important;}
        .tc-dark .text-amber-600{color:#fbbf24!important;}
        .tc-dark .text-teal-600{color:#5eead4!important;}
        .tc-dark .text-indigo-400{color:#a5b4fc!important;}
        .tc-dark .text-violet-500{color:#c4b5fd!important;}
        .tc-dark .shadow-sm{box-shadow:0 0 0 1px rgba(255,255,255,.03)!important;}
        .tc-dark .tc-input{background:#141d2c;border-color:#31405c;color:#e2e8f0;}
        .tc-dark .bg-amber-400{background-color:#d97706!important;}
        .tc-dark .bg-sky-100{background-color:rgba(14,165,233,.22)!important;}
        .tc-dark .text-sky-700{color:#7dd3fc!important;}
        .tc-dark .bg-slate-200{background-color:#243146!important;}
        .tc-dark .bg-violet-100{background-color:rgba(124,58,237,.28)!important;}
        .tc-dark .text-violet-700{color:#c4b5fd!important;}
        .tc-dark .text-rose-500{color:#fb7185!important;}
      `}</style>

      <div className="tc-shell mx-auto">
        {/* Command bar */}
        <header className="px-4 pb-3" style={{ paddingTop: "calc(1.25rem + env(safe-area-inset-top, 0px))" }}>
          <div className="flex items-center justify-between">
            <div>
              <div className="font-display text-xl font-bold text-slate-900 leading-none">Trainings-Cockpit</div>
              <div className="text-xs text-slate-400 mt-1">Volleyball · Laufen · Kraft · Schule</div>
            </div>
            <div className="flex items-center gap-2.5">
              <div className="text-right text-[11px] text-slate-400 font-num">{today.toLocaleDateString("de-DE", { weekday: "short", day: "2-digit", month: "2-digit" })}</div>
              <button onClick={() => setShowSettings((s) => !s)} aria-label="Einstellungen"
                className={`h-11 w-11 rounded-xl border flex items-center justify-center transition ${showSettings ? "bg-indigo-600 border-transparent text-white" : "bg-white border-slate-200 text-slate-500"}`}>
                <Settings size={18} />
              </button>
            </div>
          </div>
        </header>

        {/* Navigation: oben Bereiche (Training/Schule), darunter nur im Training die Unter-Tabs */}
        <nav className="sticky top-0 z-20 bg-slate-50/90 px-4 pb-2 backdrop-blur border-b border-slate-200/70 space-y-2">
          {/* Oberste Ebene: segmentierte Bereichs-Umschaltung (bewusst anders als die Indigo-Tabs darunter) */}
          <div className="flex gap-1 rounded-2xl bg-slate-100 p-1">
            {AREAS.map((a) => {
              const Icon = a.icon, active = area === a.id && !showSettings;
              return (
                <button key={a.id} onClick={() => { setArea(a.id); setShowSettings(false); }} className={`flex-1 flex items-center justify-center gap-1.5 rounded-xl py-2 transition ${active ? "bg-white shadow-sm text-indigo-700" : "text-slate-500"}`}>
                  <Icon size={16} /><span className="text-xs font-bold">{a.label}</span>
                </button>
              );
            })}
          </div>
          {/* Zweite Ebene: Trainings-Tabs, nur sichtbar wenn Bereich = Training */}
          {area === "training" && (
            <div className="flex gap-1 rounded-2xl bg-white border border-slate-200 p-1 shadow-sm">
              {TABS.map((t) => {
                const Icon = t.icon, active = tab === t.id && !showSettings;
                return (
                  <button key={t.id} onClick={() => { setTab(t.id); setShowSettings(false); }} className={`flex-1 flex flex-col items-center gap-0.5 rounded-xl py-2.5 transition ${active ? "bg-indigo-600 text-white" : "text-slate-400"}`}>
                    <Icon size={17} /><span className="text-[10px] font-semibold">{t.label}</span>
                  </button>
                );
              })}
            </div>
          )}
        </nav>

        <main className="px-4 py-4">
          {!loaded ? (
            <div className="py-20 text-center text-sm text-slate-400">Lade …</div>
          ) : showSettings ? (
            <SettingsView data={data} setData={setData} savedAt={savedAt} onRefresh={manualRefresh} refreshing={refreshing} onReset={reset} onClose={() => setShowSettings(false)} />
          ) : area === "kalender" ? (
            <CalendarTab data={data} />
          ) : area === "schule" ? (
            <SchoolTab data={data} setData={setData} />
          ) : (
            <>
              {tab === "cockpit" && <CockpitTab data={data} setData={setData} currentWeek={currentWeek} daysToT={daysToT} phaseNow={phaseNow} plan={plan} goWeek={() => setTab("woche")} goRecovery={() => setTab("recovery")} goKcal={() => setTab("kcal")} goSchule={() => { setArea("schule"); setShowSettings(false); }} tournamentPassed={tournamentPassed} />}
              {tab === "woche" && <WeekTab data={data} setData={setData} currentWeek={currentWeek} tournamentPassed={tournamentPassed} />}
              {tab === "fortschritt" && <ProgressTab data={data} setData={setData} currentWeek={currentWeek} />}
              {tab === "kcal" && <NutritionTab data={data} setData={setData} plan={plan} />}
              {tab === "recovery" && <RecoveryTab data={data} setData={setData} currentWeek={currentWeek} />}
            </>
          )}

          <footer className="mt-8 flex items-center justify-center text-[11px] text-slate-400" style={{ paddingBottom: "calc(0.5rem + env(safe-area-inset-bottom, 0px))" }}>
            <span>{savedAt ? `Zuletzt gespeichert ${savedAt.toLocaleTimeString("de-DE", { hour: "2-digit", minute: "2-digit" })} · v7.2` : "Fortschritt wird automatisch gespeichert · v7.2"}</span>
          </footer>
        </main>
      </div>
    </div>
    </ThemeContext.Provider>
  );
}
